Question #1 (ID: 414822)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board

Question:
[math]f(x)=x^{2}+3 x, g(x)=2 x-3[/math] এবং [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}3 & 1 & -1 \\2 & 3 & 4 \\-4 & 5 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]

ক . নির্ণায়কের সাহায্যে সমাধান কর : [math]x+3 y+2[/math] [math]=0,2 x+y+3=0[/math]

Options:
খ. [math]f(\Lambda)+1[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\mathrm{go} f(\mathrm{x})[/math] এর লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে[math]x+3 y+2=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x+3 y=-2[/math]
 [math]......(i)[/math]
এবং [math]2 x+y+3=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 x+y=-3[/math]
 [math]........(ii)[/math]
 [math]D=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 3 \\2 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1-6=-5[/math]
 [math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}-2 & 3 \\-3 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-2+9=7[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & -2 \\2 & -3\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-3+4=1[/math]
 [math]x=\frac{D_{x}}{D}=\frac{7}{-5}[/math]
 এবং [math]y=\frac{D_{y}}{D}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{5}[/math]
নির্ণেয় সমাধান, [math](x, y)[/math]
 [math]=\left(-\frac{7}{5},-\frac{1}{5}\right)[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]f(x)=x^{2}+3 x[/math]
 [math]\therefore f(A)=A^{2}+3 A[/math]
 [math]A^{2}=A \cdot A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 1 & -1 \\2 & 3 & 4 \\-4 & 5 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\times\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 1 & -1 \\2 & 3 & 4 \\-4 & 5 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{cc}9+2+4 & 3+3-5 \\6+6-16 & 2+9+20 \\-12+10-24 & -4+15+30\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}-3+4-6 \\-2+12+24 \\4+20+36\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{ccc}15 & 1 & -5 \\-4 & 31 & 34 \\-26 & 41 & 60\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]3 A=3\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 1 & -1 \\2 & 3 & 4 \\-4 & 5 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}9 & 3 & -3 \\6 & 9 & 12 \\-12 & 15 & 18\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]f(A)+1=\mathrm{A}^{2}[/math]
 [math]+3 \mathrm{~A}+\mathrm{I}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{ccc}15 & 1 & -5 \\-4 & 31 & 34 \\-26 & 41 & 60\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ccc}9 & 3 & -3 \\6 & 9 & 12 \\-12 & 15 & 18\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{ccc}25 & 4 & -8 \\2 & 41 & 46 \\-38 & 56 & 79\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে [math]f(x)=x^{2}+3 x[/math]
এবং [math]\mathrm{g}(\mathrm{x})[/math]
 [math]=2 \mathrm{x}-3[/math]
এখন, [math]g o f(x)=g\left(x^{2}+3 x\right)[/math]
 [math]=2\left(x^{2}+3 x\right)-3[/math]
 [math]=2 x^{2}+6 x-3[/math]
ধরি, [math]y=g o f(x)=2 x^{2}+6 x-3[/math]
 [math]x[/math]
 এর বিভিন্ন মানের জন্য [math]y[/math]
 এর সংশ্লিষ্ট মান নির্ণয় করি :
[Image]
ছক কাগজের X অক্ষ ও Y- অক্ষ বরাবর ক্ষুদ্রতম বর্গের 1 ঘর = 1 একক ধরে প্রদর বিন্দুগুলো স্থাপন স্থাপন করি। অতঃপর বিন্দুগুলো যোগ করে লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন করি :
[Image]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক সমীকরণগুলোকে Cramer-এর নিয়মে সমাধান করলে প্রথমে ধনাত্মক অক্ষগুলোর মান লিখে: [math]D=\begin{vmatrix}1&3\\[4pt]2&1\end{vmatrix}=1\cdot1-3\cdot2=-5,[/math] ধ্রুবকগুলো ডান পাশে নেওয়া গেলে [math]D_x=\begin{vmatrix}-2&3\\[4pt]-3&1\end{vmatrix}=7,\;D_y=\begin{vmatrix}1&-2\\[4pt]2&-3\end{vmatrix}=1[/math] তাই [math]x=D_x/D=-7/5,\;y=D_y/D=-1/5[/math]।

খ প্রথমে [math]\Lambda=\det A[/math] গণনা করলে একটি সারি-বিস্তারে পাওয়া যায় [math]\Lambda=-56[/math]; অতঃপর [math]f(\Lambda)+1 =(-56)^2+3(-56)+1=3136-168+1=2969[/math]।

গ সংকলন করলে [math]g\circ f(x)=g(f(x))=2(x^2+3x)-3=2x^2+6x-3[/math]; এটি একটি উর্ধ্বমুখী পরাবৃত্তি যার অক্ষসংমিতি [math]x=-\dfrac{3}{2}[/math], শীর্ষবিন্দুতে মান [math]-\dfrac{15}{2}[/math], y-ছেদক [math]-3[/math] এবং শূন্যবিন্দুগুলি [math]x=\dfrac{-3\pm\sqrt{15}}{2}[/math]।

Question #2 (ID: 414823)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x+y+z=1[/math] [math]........(i)[/math] [math]l x+m y+n z=k[/math] [math].......(ii)[/math] [math]l^{2} x+\mathrm{m}^{2} y+\mathrm{n}^{2} \mathrm{z}=\mathrm{k}^{2}[/math] [math]......(iii)[/math]

ক . [math]2\left[\begin{array}{r}1-2 \\2-1\end{array}\right]+\mathrm{F}=\mathrm{I}_{2}[/math] হলে, [math]F[/math] ম্যাট্রিক্সটি নির্ণয় কর; যেখানে, [math]\mathrm{I}_{2}[/math] একটি অভেদ ম্যাট্রিক্স ।

Options:
খ. সমীকরণগুলোকে [math]A X=B[/math] আকারে প্রকাশ করে দেখাও যে, [math]\operatorname{det}(\mathrm{A})=(l-\mathrm{m})[/math] [math](\mathrm{m}-\mathrm{n})(\mathrm{n}-l)[/math]
গ. [math]x,y,z[/math] এর সহগ নিয়ে গঠিত [math]A[/math] একটি ম্যাট্রিক্স। [math]A[/math] এর বিপরীত ম্যাট্রিক্স নির্ণয় কর; যেখানে [math]l=1, m=2,[/math] [math]n=-1 \text {. }[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\mathrm{I}_{2}=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right] ; 2\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & -2 \\2 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\mathrm{F}=\mathrm{I}_{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & -4 \\4 & -2\end{array}\right]+\mathrm{F}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow F=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right]-\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & -4 \\4 & -2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1-2 & 0+4 \\0-4 & 1+2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}-1 & 4 \\-4 & 3\end{array}\right] \text {. }[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]x+y+z=1[/math]
 [math]......(i)[/math]
 [math]l_X+m y+n z=k[/math]
 [math]......(ii)[/math]
 [math]l^{2} x+m^{2} y+n^{2} z=k^{2}[/math]
 [math]......(iii)[/math]
এখানে, [math]A x=B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\l & m & n \\l^{2} & m^{2} & n^{2}\end{array}\right)\left(\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\left(\begin{array}{c}1 \\k \\k^{2}\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]\operatorname{det}(A)=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\l & m & n \\l^{2} & m^{2} & n^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}0 & 0 & 1 \\l-m & m-n & n \\l^{2}-m^{2} & m^{2}-n^{2} & n^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}c_{1}^{\prime}=c_{1}-c_{2} \\c_{2}^{\prime}=c_{2}-c_{2}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left|\begin{array}{cc}l-m & m-n \\l^{2}-m^{2} & m^{2}-n^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (l-m)(m-n)\left|\begin{array}{cc}1 & 1 \\l+\mathrm{m} & \mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(l-m)(m-n)(m+n-l-m)[/math]
 [math]=(l-m)(m-n)(n-l)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \operatorname{det}(\Lambda)=(l-m)(\mathrm{m}-\mathrm{n})(\mathrm{n}-l)[/math]
 দেখানো হলোগ [math]x, y, z[/math]
 এর সহগ নিয়ে গঠিত [math]A[/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্স[math]\mathrm{A}=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\l & \mathrm{~m} & \mathrm{n} \\\mathrm{l}_{2} & \mathrm{~m}^{2} & \mathrm{n}^{2}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]|A|=1(2+4)--1(1+1)+1(4-2)[/math]
 [math]=6-2+2=6[/math]
 [math]|A|[/math]
 এর সহগুণকসমূহ[math]A_{11}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}2 & -1 \\4 & 1\end{array}\right|=2+4=6[/math]
 [math]A_{12}=-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -1 \\1 & 1\end{array}\right|=-(1,+1)=-2[/math]
 [math]A_{13}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\1 & 4\end{array}\right|=4-2=2[/math]
 [math]A_{21}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\4 & 1\end{array}\right|=-(1-4)=3[/math]
 [math]{A_{22}}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\1 & 1\end{array}\right|=1-1=0[/math]
 [math]A_{23}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\1 & 4\end{array}\right|=-(4-1)=-3[/math]
 [math]A_{31}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 1 \\2 & -1\end{array}\right|=-1-2=-3[/math]
 [math]A_{32}=-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 1 \\1 & -1\end{array}\right|=-(-1-1)=2[/math]
 [math]A_{33}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|=2-1=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \operatorname{Adj} A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}6 & -2 & 2 \\3 & 0 & -3 \\-3 & 2 & 1\end{array}\right]^T[/math]
 [math]A[/math]
 এর বিপরীত ম্যাট্রিক্স , [math]A^{-1}=\frac{\operatorname{Adj} A}{|A|}=\frac{1}{6}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}6 & -2 & -2 \\3 & 0 & -3 \\-3 & 2 & 1\end{array}\right]^{T}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{6}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}6 & 3 & -3 \\-2 & 0 & 2 \\2 & -3 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]


Explanation:
ক  সমীকরণ থেকে [math]2\begin{pmatrix}1 & -2\\[4pt]2 & -1\end{pmatrix}=\begin{pmatrix}2 & -4\\[4pt]4 & -2\end{pmatrix}[/math], তাই [math]F=I_2-2\begin{pmatrix}1 & -2\\[4pt]2 & -1\end{pmatrix}=\begin{pmatrix}-1 & 4\\[4pt]-4 & 3\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

খ  সমীকরণগুলোকে [math]A X=B[/math] আকারে লিখলে [math]A=\begin{pmatrix}1&1&1\\[4pt]l&m&n\\[4pt]l^2&m^2&n^2\end{pmatrix}[/math] হয়, যা Vandermonde ম্যাট্রিক্স; তার ডিটারমিন্যান্ট হল [math]\prod_{1\le iগ  l=1, m=2, n=-1 হলে [math]A=\begin{pmatrix}1&1&1\\[4pt]1&2&-1\\[4pt]1&4&1\end{pmatrix}[/math], [math]\det A=6[/math] এবং সরল হিসাব/adjoint ব্যবহার করে  
[math]A^{-1}=\frac{1}{6}\begin{pmatrix}6&3&-3\\[4pt]-2&0&2\\[4pt]2&-3&1\end{pmatrix}=\begin{pmatrix}1&\tfrac{1}{2}&-\tfrac{1}{2}\\[4pt]-\tfrac{1}{3}&0&\tfrac{1}{3}\\[4pt]\tfrac{1}{3}&-\tfrac{1}{2}&\tfrac{1}{6}\end{pmatrix}[/math] ।

Question #3 (ID: 414824)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 2 & -3 \\-2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{cc}-1 & 2 \\-3 & 7 \\5 & 0\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{cc}5 & 1 \\1 & -3\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]D=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & -1 \\0 & -2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]X[/math]-এর যেসব মানের জন্য [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}x^{2} & 2 x \\5 & 3\end{array}\right][/math] ম্যাট্রিক্স ব্যতিক্রমী হবে তা নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]\mathrm{AB}-\mathrm{C}^{2}+2 \mathrm{I}_{2}[/math] নির্ণয় করা
গ. [math]\mathrm{D}^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}x^{2} & 2 x \\5 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 ব্যতিক্রমী, ম্যাট্রিক হবে যদি [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}x^{2} & 2 x \\5 & 3\end{array}\right|=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 x^{2}-10 x=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x(3 x-10)=0[/math]
হয় [math]x=0[/math]
অথবা, [math]3 x-10=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 x=10[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x=\frac{10}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x[/math]
 এর মান [math]0, \frac{10}{3} \text {. }[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & -3 \\-2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right] ;[/math]
 [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{rr}-1 & 2 \\-3 & 7 \\5 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
এবং [math]{C}=\left[\begin{array}{rr}5 & 1 \\1 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
এখন, [math]A B=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & -3 \\-2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\times\left[\begin{array}{rr}-1 & 2 \\-3 & 7 \\5 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\mathrm{C}^{2}=\mathrm{C} \cdot \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}5 & 1 \\1 & -3\end{array}\right] \cdot\left[\begin{array}{cc}5 & 1 \\1 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}25+1 & 5-3 \\5-3 & 1+9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}26 & 2 \\2 & 10\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]I_{2}=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]2 \mathrm{I}_{2}=2\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\0 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি: [math]=\mathrm{AB}-\mathrm{C}^{2}+2 \mathrm{~I}_{2}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}-22 & 16 \\-1 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{cc}26 & 2 \\2 &10\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\0 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cr}-48 & 14 \\-3 & -7\end{array}\right]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\0 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}-46 & 14 \\-3 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]D=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & -1 \\0 & -2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]D_{11}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}-2 & 2 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|=-6-4=-10[/math]
 [math]D_{12}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 2 \\1 & 3\end{array}\right|=-(0-2)=2[/math]
 [math]D_{13}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}0 & -2 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|=0+2=2[/math]
 [math]D_{21}=-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -1 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|=-(3+2)=-5[/math]
 [math]D_{22}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -1 \\1 & 3\end{array}\right|=3+1=4[/math]
 [math]D_{23}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(2-1)=-1[/math]
 [math]D_{31}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -1 \\-2 & \end{array}\right|=2-2=0[/math]
 [math]D_{32}=-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -1 \\0 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(2+0)=-2[/math]
 [math]D_{33}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 1 \\0 & -2\end{array}\right|=-2-0=-2[/math]
 [math]\text { Adj } D=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-10 & 2 & 2 \\-5 & 4 & -1 \\0 & -2 & -2\end{array}\right]^{T}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad D^{-1}=\frac{A d j D}{|D|}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{10}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-10 & 2 & 2 \\-5 & 4 & -1 \\0 & -2 & -2\end{array}\right]^{\top}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{10}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-10 & -5 & 0 \\2 & 4 & -2 \\2 & -1 & -2\end{array}\right][/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক ম্যাট্রিক্স ব্যতিক্রমী (singular) হওয়ার শর্ত হলো নির্ণায়ক শূন্য হওয়া; এখানে [math]\det\begin{pmatrix}x^2 & 2x\\[4pt]5 & 3\end{pmatrix}=3x^2-10x=x(3x-10)[/math], তাই [math]x=0[/math] বা [math]x=\tfrac{10}{3}[/math] হলে ব্যতিক্রমী হবে।

খ প্রথমে [math]AB=\begin{pmatrix}-22 & 16\\[4pt]-1 & 3\end{pmatrix}[/math], [math]C^2=\begin{pmatrix}26 & 2\\[4pt]2 & 10\end{pmatrix}[/math] এবং [math]2I_2=\begin{pmatrix}2 & 0\\[4pt]0 & 2\end{pmatrix}[/math]; তাই [math]AB-C^2+2I_2=\begin{pmatrix}-46 & 14\\[4pt]-3 & -5\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

গ প্রথমে [math]\det D=-10[/math] পাই; এরপর সহগীয় (adjugate) ব্যবহার করে [math]D^{-1}=\dfrac{1}{-10}\operatorname{adj}(D)=\begin{pmatrix}1 & \tfrac{1}{2} & 0\\[4pt]-\tfrac{1}{5} & -\tfrac{2}{5} & \tfrac{1}{5}\\[4pt]-\tfrac{1}{5} & \tfrac{1}{10} & \tfrac{1}{5}\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

Question #4 (ID: 414825)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 3 & 1 \\1 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right], B=A^{t}, f(x)=x^{2}-4 x[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]g(x)=\frac{1}{2 x-3}[/math] ফাংশনটির রেঞ্জ নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]f(\mathrm{~B})[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. B এর বিপরীত ম্যাট্রিক্স নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]g(x)=\frac{1}{2 x-3}[/math]
ধরি, [math]g(x)=y[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{ll}\therefore & \mathrm{y}=\frac{1}{2 x-3} \\\Rightarrow & 2 x y-3 y=1 \\\Rightarrow & 2 x y=1+3 y \\\Rightarrow & x=\frac{1+3 y}{2 y} \\\Rightarrow & g^{-1}(y)=\frac{1+3 y}{2 y} \\\therefore & g^{-1}(x)=\frac{1+3 x}{2 x}\end{array}[/math]
কিন্তু, [math]2 x 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad g(\mathbf{x})[/math]
 রেঞ্জ [math]\mathbf{R}-\{0\}[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 3 & 1 \\1 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right] ;[/math]
 [math]A^{\mathrm{t}}=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
এবং [math]f(x)=x^{2}-4 x[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad f(B)=B^{2}-4[/math]
 [math]B=\left(A^{t}\right)^{2}-4 A^{t}\left[B=A^{t}\right][/math]
 [math]\left(A^{t}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=A^{t} \cdot A^{t}=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}4+3+1 & 2+2+2 \\6+6+2 & 3+4+4 \\2+6+0 & 1+4+0\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{l}2+2+0 \\3+4+0 \\1+4+0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}8 & 6 & 4 \\14 & 11 & 7 \\8 & 5 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
এবং [math]4 A^{t}=4\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}8 & 4 & 4 \\12 & 8 & 8 \\4 & 8 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore f(B)=\left(A^{t}\right)^{2}-4 A^{t}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{ccc}8 & 6 & 4 \\14 & 11 & 7 \\8 & 5 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ccc}8 & 4 & 4 \\12 & 8 & 8 \\4 & 8 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}0 & 2 & 0 \\2 & 3 & -1 \\4 & -3 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 গ [math]\begin{aligned}B & =A^{t}=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right] \\|B| & =2(0-4)-1(0-2)+1(6-2) \\& =-8+2+4=-2\end{aligned}[/math]
B এর সহগুণকসমূহ :[math]\begin{aligned}B_{11} & =\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 2 \\2 & 0\end{array}\right|=0-4=-4 \\B_{12} & =-\left|\begin{array}{ll}3 & 2 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right|=-(0-2)=2 \\B_{13} & =\left|\begin{array}{ll}3 & 2 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|=6-2=4 \\B_{21} & =-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\2 & 0\end{array}\right|=-(0-2)=2 \\B_{22} & =\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right|=0-1=-1 \\B_{23} & =-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(4-1)=-3 \\B_{31} & =\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\2 & 2\end{array}\right|=2-2=0 \\B_{32} & =-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\3 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(4-3)=-1 \\B_{33} & =\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\3 & 2\end{array}\right|=4-3=1\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\operatorname{Adj} B=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-4 & 2 & 4 \\2 & -1 & -3 \\0 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right]^{T}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-4 & 2 & 0 \\2 & -1 & -1 \\4 & -3 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad B^{-1}=\frac{\text { Adj } B}{|B|}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-4 & 2 & 0 \\2 & -1 & -1 \\4 & -3 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক ফাংশনটি [math]y=\dfrac{1}{2x-3}[/math] থেকে [math]y=0[/math] হলে কোনো সমাধান নেই (বাম পাশে শূন্য হতে পারে না), এবং যেকোনো [math]y\neq0[/math] জন্য [math]x=\dfrac{1/y+3}{2}[/math] পাওয়া যায়, সুতরাং রেঞ্জ হলো [math]\mathbb{R}\setminus\{0\}[/math]।

খ প্রথমে [math]B=A^{t}=\begin{pmatrix}2&1&1\\3&2&2\\1&2&0\end{pmatrix}[/math], এরপর [math]B^{2}=\begin{pmatrix}8&6&4\\14&11&7\\8&5&5\end{pmatrix}[/math] এবং [math]4B=\begin{pmatrix}8&4&4\\12&8&8\\4&8&0\end{pmatrix}[/math], তাই [math]f(B)=B^{2}-4B=\begin{pmatrix}0&2&0\\2&3&-1\\4&-3&5\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

গ ডিটারমিন্যান্ট গণনা করলে [math]\det B=-2\neq0[/math], তাই বিপরীত আছে; কোফ্যাক্টর-বর্তনী প্রয়োগে পাওয়া যায় [math]B^{-1}=\begin{pmatrix}2&-1&0\\-1&\tfrac{1}{2}&\tfrac{1}{2}\\-2&\tfrac{3}{2}&-\tfrac{1}{2}\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

Question #5 (ID: 414826)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 4 & 2 \\4 & 0 & 3 \\2 & 3 & 2\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{l}2 \\5 \\4\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]A \times C[/math] নির্ণয় করে উহার মাত্রা নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\mathrm{A}^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]A \times B=C[/math] হলে, ক্রেমারের নিয়মে সমীকরণ জোটটির সমাধান কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে , [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 4 & 2 \\4 & 0 & 3 \\2 & 3 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{C}=\left[\begin{array}{l}2 \\5 \\4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]A \times C=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 4 & 2 \\4 & 0 & 3 \\2 & 3 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\times\left[\begin{array}{l}2 \\5 \\4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{l}1 \times 2+4 \times 5+2 \times 4 \\4 \times 2+0 \times 5+3 \times 4 \\2 \times 2+3 \times 5+2 \times 4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}2+20+8 \\8+0+12 \\4+15+8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}30 \\20 \\27\end{array}\right]_{3 \times 1}[/math]
 [math]A \times C[/math]
 এর মাত্রা [math]3 \times 1 \text {. }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে , [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 4 & 2 \\4 & 0 & 3 \\2 & 3 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]|A|=1(0-9)-4(8-6)[/math]
 [math]+2(12-0)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow-9-8+24=-17+24=7[/math]
A এর সহগুণকসমূহ :[math]\begin{array}{l}A_{11}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 3 \\3 & 2\end{array}\right|=0-9=-9 \\A_{12}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}4 & 3 \\2 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(8-6)=-2 \\A_{13}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}4 & 0 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|=12-0=12 \\A_{21}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\3 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(8-6)=-2 \\A_{22}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\2 & 2\end{array}\right|=2-4=-2 \\A_{23}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 4 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|=-(3-8)=5 \\A_{31}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\0 & 3\end{array}\right|=12-0=12 \\A_{32}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\4 & 3\end{array}\right|=-(3-8)=5 \\A_{33}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 4 \\4 & 0\end{array}\right|=0-16=-16\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\text { Adj } A=\left[\begin{array}{rrc}-9 & -2 & 12 \\-2 & -2 & 5 \\12 & 5 & -16\end{array}\right]^{T}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-9 & -2 & 12 \\-2 & -2 & 5 \\12 & 5 & -16\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad A^{-1}=\frac{\text { Adj } A}{|A|}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{7}\left[\begin{array}{rrc}-9 & -2 & 12 \\-2 & -2 & 5 \\12 & 5 & -16\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\mathrm{A} \times \mathrm{B}=\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 4 & 2 \\4 & 0 & 3 \\2 & 3 & 2\end{array}\right] \times\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}2 \\5 \\4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{c}x+4 y+2 z \\4 x+0+3 z \\2 x+3 y+2 z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}2 \\5 \\4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow x+4 y+2 z=2 \\4 x+0+3 z=5 \\2 x+3 y+2 z=4\end{array}[/math]
x, y ও z-এর সহগগুলো নিয়ে গঠিত নির্ণায়ক[math]D=\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & 4 & 2 \\4 & 0 & 3 \\2 & 3 & 2\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1(0-9)-4(8-6)+2(12-0)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow-9-8+24=7[/math]
 [math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{lll}2 & 4 & 2 \\5 & 0 & 3 \\4 & 3 & 2\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2(0-9)-4(10-12)[/math]
 [math]+2(15-0)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow-18+8+30=20[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & 2 & 2 \\4 & 5 & 3 \\2 & 4 & 2\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1(10-12)-2(8-6)[/math]
 [math]+2(16-10)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow-2-4+12=6[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{D}_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & 4 & 2 \\4 & 0 & 5 \\2 & 3 & 4\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1(0-15)-4(16-10)[/math]
 [math]+2(12-0)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow-15-24+24=-15[/math]
 [math]x=\frac{D_{x}}{D}=\frac{20}{7}, y=\frac{D_{y}}{D}=\frac{6}{7}[/math]
 এবং [math]z=\frac{D_{z}}{D}=\frac{-15}{7}[/math]
নির্ণেয় সমীকরণ জোটটির সমাধান [math](x, y, z)=\left(\frac{20}{7}, \frac{6}{7}, \frac{-15}{7}\right)[/math]


Explanation:
সমাধান:

ক [math]A\times C=\begin{pmatrix}1&4&2\\4&0&3\\2&3&2\end{pmatrix}\begin{pmatrix}2\\5\\4\end{pmatrix}=\begin{pmatrix}30\\20\\27\end{pmatrix}[/math], তাই উহার মাত্রা [math]3\times1[/math]।

খ প্রথমে [math]\det A=7[/math] (অতএব উল্টানো আছে), এবং [math]\operatorname{adj}A=\begin{pmatrix}-9&-2&12\\-2&-2&5\\12&5&-16\end{pmatrix}[/math], তাই [math]A^{-1}=\dfrac{1}{7}\begin{pmatrix}-9&-2&12\\-2&-2&5\\12&5&-16\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

গ যেহেতু [math]\det A=7\neq0[/math], সমাধান একক; [math]B=A^{-1}C=\dfrac{1}{7}\begin{pmatrix}-9&-2&12\\-2&-2&5\\12&5&-16\end{pmatrix}\begin{pmatrix}2\\5\\4\end{pmatrix}=\begin{pmatrix}20/7\\6/7\\-15/7\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

Question #6 (ID: 414827)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & -3 \\-2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{rr}-1 & 2 \\-3 & 7 \\5 & 0\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{rr}5 & 1 \\1 & -3\end{array}\right], D=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & -1 \\0 & -2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]x[/math] -এর যেসব মানের জন্য [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}x^{2} & 2 x \\5 & 3\end{array}\right][/math] ম্যাট্রিক্স ব্যতিক্রমী হবে তা নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]\mathrm{AB}-\mathrm{C}^{2}+2 \mathrm{I}_{2}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\mathrm{D}^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}x^{2} & 2 x \\5 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 ব্যতিক্রমী ম্যাট্রিক হবে যদি [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}x^{2} & 2 x \\5 & 3\end{array}\right|=0[/math]
 হয়[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 3 x^{2}-10 x=0\\\Rightarrow x(3 x-10)=0 \text{,}\\\Rightarrow x=0\end{array}[/math]
অথবা [math]3 x-10=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 x=10\Rightarrow x=\frac{10}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x[/math]
 এর মান [math]0, \frac{10}{3}[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে , [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & -3 \\-2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right] ;[/math]
 [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{rr}-1 & 2 \\-3 & 7 \\5 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
এবং [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{cc}5 & 1 \\1 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
এখন [math]A B=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & -3 \\-2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\times\left[\begin{array}{rr}-1 & 2 \\-3 & 7 \\5 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rr}-1-6-15 & 2+14+0 \\2-3+0 & -4+7+0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}-22 & 16 \\-1 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]C^{2}=C \cdot C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}5 & 1 \\1 & -3\end{array}\right] \cdot\left[\begin{array}{cc}5 & 1 \\1 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}25+1 & 5-3 \\5-3 & 1+9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}26 & 2 \\2 & 10\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}I_{2}=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right] \\2 I_{2}=2\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\0 & 2\end{array}\right]\end{array}[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=A B-C^{2}+2 \mathrm{I}_{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{cc}-22 & 16 \\-1 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{cc}26 & 2 \\2 & 10\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\0 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rr}-48 & 14 \\-3 & -7\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\0 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}-46 & 14 \\-3 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]D=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & -1 \\0 & -2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}|D| & =1(-6-4)-1(0-2)-1(0+2) \\& \Rightarrow-10+2-2=-10\end{aligned}[/math]
D-এর সহগুণকসমূহ :[math]\begin{array}{l}D_{11}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}-2 & 2 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|=-6-4=-10 \\D_{12}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 2 \\1 & 3\end{array}\right|=-(0-2)=2 \\D_{13}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}0 & -2 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|=0+2=2\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}D_{21}=-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -1 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|=-(3+2)=-5 \\D_{22}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -1 \\1 & 3\end{array}\right|=3+1=4 \\D_{23}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(2-1)=-1 \\D_{31}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -1 \\-2 & 2\end{array}\right|=2-2=0 \\D_{32}=-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -1 \\0 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(2+0)=-2 \\D_{33}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 1 \\0 & -2\end{array}\right|=-2-0=-2\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\operatorname{Adj} D=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-10 & 2 & 2 \\-5 & 4 & -1 \\0 & -2 & -2\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{T}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad D^{-1}=\frac{\text { Adj D }}{|D|}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -\frac{1}{10}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-10 & 2 & 2 \\-5 & 4 & -1 \\0 & -2 & -2\end{array}\right]^T[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{10}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-10 & -5 & 0 \\2 & 4 & -2 \\2 & -1 & -2\end{array}\right][/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক  কোন ম্যাট্রিক্স ব্যতিক্রমী (singular) হলে তার ডিটারমিন্যান্ট শূন্য হয়; এখানে [math]\det\begin{pmatrix}x^2&2x\\5&3\end{pmatrix}=3x^2-10x=x(3x-10)[/math], তাই [math]x=0[/math] অথবা [math]x=\tfrac{10}{3}[/math] এ ম্যাট্রিক্স ব্যতিক্রমী হবে।

খ  প্রথমে [math]AB=\begin{pmatrix}-22&16\\-1&3\end{pmatrix}[/math], [math]C^2=\begin{pmatrix}26&2\\2&10\end{pmatrix}[/math] এবং [math]2I_2=\begin{pmatrix}2&0\\0&2\end{pmatrix}[/math]। তাই [math]AB-C^2+2I_2=\begin{pmatrix}-46&14\\-3&-5\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

গ  প্রথমে [math]\det D=-10\neq0[/math], সুতরাং inverse আছে; কোফ্যাক্টর-ম্যাট্রিক্সের অ্যাডজুগেট নেওয়ার পরে [math]D^{-1}=\frac{1}{-10}\begin{pmatrix}-10&-5&0\\2&4&-2\\2&-1&-2\end{pmatrix}=\begin{pmatrix}1&\tfrac{1}{2}&0\\[4pt]-\tfrac{1}{5}&-\tfrac{2}{5}&\tfrac{1}{5}\\[4pt]-\tfrac{1}{5}&\tfrac{1}{10}&\tfrac{1}{5}\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

Question #7 (ID: 414828)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{A}=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 3 & 1 \\1 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right], \mathrm{B}=\mathrm{A}^{\mathrm{t}}, f(\mathrm{x})=\mathrm{x}^{2}-4 \mathrm{x}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]g(x)=\frac{1}{2 x-3}[/math] - ফাংশনটির রেঞ্জ নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]f(\mathrm{~B})[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
গ. [math]B[/math] এর বিপরীত ম্যাট্রিক্স নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]g(x)=\frac{1}{2 x-3}[/math]
ধরি, [math]g(x)=y[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{ll}\therefore & y=\frac{1}{2 x-3} \\\Rightarrow & 2 x y-3 y=1 \\\Rightarrow & 2 x y=1+3 y \\\Rightarrow & x=\frac{1+3 y}{2 y} \\\Rightarrow & g^{-1}(y)=\frac{1+3 y}{2 y} \\\therefore & g^{-1}(x)=\frac{1+3 x}{2 x}\end{array}[/math]
কিন্তু [math]2 x 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad g(x)[/math]
 রেঞ্জ [math]\mathbb{R}-\{0\}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 3 & 1 \\1 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right] ;[/math]
 [math]A^{t}=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
এবং [math]f(x)=x^{2}-4 x[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad f(B)=B^{2}-4 B[/math]
 [math]=\left(A^{t}\right)^{2}-4 A^{t}\left[B=A^{t}\right][/math]
 [math]\left(A^{t}\right)^{2}=A^{t} \cdot A^{t}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}4+3+1 & 2+2+2 \\6+6+2 & 3+4+4 \\2+6+0 & 1+4+0\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}2+2+0 \\3+4+0 \\1+4+0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}8 & 6 & 4 \\14 & 11 & 7 \\8 & 5 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
এবং [math]4 A^{t}=4\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}8 & 4 & 4 \\12 & 8 & 8 \\4 & 8 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore f(B)=\left(A^{t}\right)^{2}-4 A^{t}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ccc}8 & 6 & 4 \\14 & 11 & 7 \\8 & 5 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ccc}8 & 4 & 4 \\12 & 8 & 8 \\4 & 8 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}0 & 2 & 0 \\2 & 3 & -1 \\4 & -3 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]B=A^{t}=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 1 & 1 \\3 & 2 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]|B|=2(0-4)-1(0-2)[/math]
 [math]+1(6-2)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow-8+2+4=-2[/math]
B এর সহগুণকসমূহ :[math]\begin{array}{l}B_{11}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 2 \\2 & 0\end{array}\right|=0-4=-4 \\B_{12}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}3 & 2 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right|=-(0-2)=2 \\B_{13}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}3 & 2 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|=6-2=4 \\B_{21}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\2 & 0\end{array}\right|=-(0-2)=2 \\B_{22}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right|=0-1=-1 \\B_{23}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(4-1)=-3 \\B_{31}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\2 & 2\end{array}\right|=2-2=0 \\B_{32}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\3 & 2\end{array}\right|=-(4-3)=-1 \\B_{33}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\3 & 2\end{array}\right|=4-3=1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\text { Adj } B=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-4 & 2 & 4 \\2 & -1 & -3 \\0 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{T}}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-4 & 2 & 0 \\2 & -1 & -1 \\4 & -3 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad B^{-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\text { AdjB }}{|\mathrm{B}|}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-4 & 2 & 0 \\2 & -1 & -1 \\4 & -3 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]g(x)=\frac{1}{2x-3}[/math] ফাংশনের রেঞ্জ সব বাস্তব সংখ্যা শূন্য ব্যতীত, কারণ [math]y=\frac{1}{2x-3}[/math] থেকে [math]x=\frac{3+1/y}{2}[/math] লিখলে দেখা যায় [math]y\neq0[/math]; তাই রেঞ্জ = [math]\mathbb{R}\setminus\{0\}[/math]।

খ [math]B=A^{\mathrm{t}}=[\begin{smallmatrix}2&1&1\\3&2&2\\1&2&0\end{smallmatrix}][/math] এবং [math]f(B)=B^{2}-4B[/math] হিসেব করলে ফল পাওয়া যায় [math]f(B)=[\begin{smallmatrix}0&2&0\\2&3&-1\\4&-3&5\end{smallmatrix}][/math] (এখানে প্রথমে [math]B^{2}[/math] গণনা করে তার থেকে [math]4B[/math] বিয়োগ করা হয়েছে)।

গ [math]\det A=-2\neq0[/math] হওয়ায় বিপরীত রয়েছে; [math]A^{-1}=\frac{1}{-2}\operatorname{adj}(A)=[\begin{smallmatrix}2&-1&-2\\-1&\tfrac{1}{2}&\tfrac{3}{2}\\0&\tfrac{1}{2}&-\tfrac{1}{2}\end{smallmatrix}][/math], তাই [math]B^{-1}=(A^{-1})^{\mathrm{t}}=[\begin{smallmatrix}2&-1&0\\-1&\tfrac{1}{2}&\tfrac{1}{2}\\-2&\tfrac{3}{2}&-\tfrac{1}{2}\end{smallmatrix}][/math]।

Question #8 (ID: 414829)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{A}=\left[\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\3 & 5\end{array}\right] ; \mathrm{B}=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\1\end{array}\right] \text { এবং } \mathrm{X}=\left[\begin{array}{c}x \\\dot{y}\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]p[/math] এর মান কত হলে [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}p-2 & 3 \\4 & 5\end{array}\right][/math] একটি ব্যতিক্রমী বৰ্গ ম্যাট্রিক্স হবে ?
খ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে, [math]A^{2}-5 A+6 I[/math] নির্ণয় কর , যেখানে, [math]I=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math] ।
গ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে, [math]A X=B[/math] হলে ক্রেমার পদ্ধতিতে [math]x,y[/math] নির্ণয় কর


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}p-2 & 3 \\4 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 একটি ব্যতিক্রমী বর্গ ম্যাট্রিক্স হবে যদি[math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}p-2 & 3 \\4 & 5\end{array}\right|=0[/math]
 হয়[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 5(p-2)-12=0 \\\Rightarrow 5 p-10-12=0 \\\Rightarrow 5 \mathrm{p}-22=0 \\\Rightarrow 5 \mathrm{p}=22 \\\therefore \quad \mathrm{p}=\frac{22}{5}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore{\mathrm{p}}[/math]
 এর মান [math]=\frac{22}{5}[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে , [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\3 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]A^{2}=A \cdot A=\left[\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\3 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\times\left[\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\3 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}16+6 & 8+10 \\12+15 & 6+25\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}22 & 18 \\27 & 31\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}5 A=5\left[\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\3 & 5\end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}20 & 10 \\15 & 25\end{array}\right] \\6 I=6\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}6 & 0 \\0 & 6\end{array}\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad A^{2}-5 A+6 I=\left[\begin{array}{ll}22 & 18 \\27 & 31\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ll}20 & 10 \\15 & 25\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}6 & 0 \\0 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 8 \\12 & 6\end{array}\right]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}6 & 0 \\0 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}8 & 8 \\12 & 12\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]A x=B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\3 & 5\end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 x+2 y=6 \\3 x+5 y=1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad D=\left|\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\3 & 5\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=20-6=14[/math]
 [math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}6 & 2 \\1 & 5\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=30-2=28[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}4 & 6 \\3 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=4-18=-14[/math]
 [math]{x}=\frac{D_{x}}{D}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{28}{14}=2[/math]
 এবং [math]y=\frac{D_{y}}{D}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-14}{14}=-1[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক অবশিষ্টতা নির্ধারণের জন্য ম্যাট্রিক্সটির নির্ণায়ক শূন্য না হওয়া চাই, তাই [math]\det\begin{pmatrix}p-2&3\\4&5\end{pmatrix}=5(p-2)-12=5p-22\neq0[/math], অর্থাৎ [math]p\neq\frac{22}{5}[/math]।

খ সরাসরি গুন এবং যোগ করলে [math]A^{2}=\begin{pmatrix}22&18\\27&31\end{pmatrix}[/math], তাই [math]A^{2}-5A+6I=\begin{pmatrix}22&18\\27&31\end{pmatrix}-\begin{pmatrix}20&10\\15&25\end{pmatrix}+\begin{pmatrix}6&0\\0&6\end{pmatrix}=\begin{pmatrix}8&8\\12&12\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

গ Cramer পদ্ধতিতে [math]\det A=4\cdot5-2\cdot3=14[/math], [math]\det A_x=\det\begin{pmatrix}6&2\\1&5\end{pmatrix}=28[/math], [math]\det A_y=\det\begin{pmatrix}4&6\\3&1\end{pmatrix}=-14[/math], তাই [math]x=\dfrac{28}{14}=2,\ y=\dfrac{-14}{14}=-1[/math]।

Question #9 (ID: 414830)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]M=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\left[\begin{array}{cr}2 & -x \\y-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math] [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rr}2 & 3+y \\4 & 2\end{array}\right][/math] হলে [math](x, y)[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]M^{2}-3 M+M I[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর, যেখানে [math]I[/math] একক ম্যাট্রিক্স ।
গ. [math]M[/math] এর বিপরীত ম্যাট্রিক্স বিদ্যমান থাকলে তা নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & -x \\y-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 3+y \\4 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}-x=3+y . . .(i) \\y-1=4 . . .(i i)\end{array}[/math]
(ii) নং হতে পাই,[math]y=1+4=5[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad y=5[/math]
y এর মান (i) নং সমীকরণ বসিয়ে পাই,[math]-x=3+5[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{ll}\therefore & x=-8 \\\therefore & (x, y)=(-8,5) .\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]M=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]M^{2}=M \cdot M[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\times\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}1+6+2 & 2-6+1 \\3-9-2 & 6+9-1 \\2+3+0 & 4-3+0\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{l}1-2+0 \\3+3-0 \\2-1+0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rrr}9 & -3 & -1 \\-8 & 14 & 6 \\5 & 1 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]3 M=3\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 6 & 3 \\9 & -9 & -3 \\6 & 3 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]M I \Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}1+0+0 & 0+2+0 \\3+0+0 & 0-3+0 \\2+0+0 & 0+1+0\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{l}0+0+1 \\0+0-1 \\0+0+0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore M^{2}-3 M+M I[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rrr}9 & -3 & -1 \\-8 & 14 & 6 \\5 & 1 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 6 & 3 \\9 & -9 & -3 \\6 & 3 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right] .[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ccc}6 & -9 & -4 \\-17 & 23 & 9 \\-1 & -2 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{crr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}7 & -7 & -3 \\-14 & 20 & 8 \\1 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে , [math]M=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 1 \\3 & -3 & -1 \\2 & 1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad|M|=1(0+1)-2(0+2)[/math]
 [math]+1(3+6)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1-4+9=6[/math]
 [math]M[/math]
 এর সহগুণকসমূহ :[math]M_{11}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}-3 & -1 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=0+1=1[/math]
 [math]M_{12}=-\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & -1 \\2 & 0\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-(0+2)=-2[/math]
 [math]M_{13}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & -3 \\2 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=3+6=9[/math]
 [math]M_{21}=-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-(0-1)=1[/math]
 [math]M_{22}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 1 \\2 & 0\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=0-2=-2[/math]
 [math]M_{23}=\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\2 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-(1-4)=3[/math]
 [math]M_{31}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}2 & 1 \\-3 & -1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-2+3=1[/math]
 [math]M_{32}=-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 1 \\3 & -1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-(-1-3)=4[/math]
 [math]M_{33}=\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 2 \\3 & -3\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-3-6=-9[/math]
 [math]\operatorname{Adj} M=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -2 & 9 \\1 & -2 & 3 \\1 & 4 & -9\end{array}\right]^{T}[/math]
 [math]M[/math]
 এর বিপরীত ম্যাট্রিক্স [math]M^{-1}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{|M|} \operatorname{Adj} M[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{6}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -2 & 9 \\1 & -2 & 3 \\1 & 4 & -9\end{array}\right]^{T}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{6}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & 1 \\-2 & -2 & 4 \\9 & 3 & -9\end{array}\right][/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক সমমিতি থেকে উপাদানগুলো মিলিয়ে: [math]y-1=4\Rightarrow y=5[/math] এবং [math]-x=3+y\Rightarrow x=-3-y=-8[/math], সুতরাং [math](x,y)=(-8,5)[/math]।

খ কারণ [math]MI=M[/math], তাই [math]M^{2}-3M+MI=M^{2}-2M[/math]। এখানে [math]M^{2}=\begin{bmatrix}9 & -3 & -1\\-8 & 14 & 6\\5 & 1 & 1\end{bmatrix}[/math] এবং [math]2M=\begin{bmatrix}2 & 4 & 2\\6 & -6 & -2\\4 & 2 & 0\end{bmatrix}[/math], তাই ফলাফল [math]M^{2}-2M=\begin{bmatrix}7 & -7 & -3\\-14 & 20 & 8\\1 & -1 & 1\end{bmatrix}[/math]।

গ নির্ণায়ক গণনা করলে [math]\det M=6\neq0[/math], তাই বিপরীত ম্যাট্রিক্স বিদ্যমান; এটি হচ্ছে [math]M^{-1}=\frac{1}{6}\begin{bmatrix}1 & 1 & 1\\-2 & -2 & 4\\9 & 3 & -9\end{bmatrix}[/math]।

Question #10 (ID: 414831)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}2 & 3 & -4 \\1 & 0 & -2 \\1 & -5 & 6\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}15 & 2 & -2 \\4 & 5 & -4 \\-5 & 3 & 7\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]2 A+3 C[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm{AC} \neq \mathrm{CA}[/math]
গ. [math]A B=\left[\begin{array}{l}1 \\3 \\2\end{array}\right][/math] হলে নির্ণায়ক পদ্ধতিতে [math]x, y[/math] ও [math]z[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]=2 \mathrm{~A}+3 \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=2\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 3 & -4 \\1 & 0 & -2 \\1 & -5 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+3\left[\begin{array}{rrr}5 & 2 & -2 \\4 & 5 & -4 \\-5 & 3 & 7\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}4 & 6 & -8 \\2 & 0 & -4 \\2 & -10 & 12\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{rrr}15 & 6 & -6 \\12 & 15 & -12 \\-15 & 9 & 21\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}4+15 & 6+6 & -8-6 \\2+12 & 0+15 & -4-12 \\2-15 & -10+9 & 12+21\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}19 & 12 & -14 \\14 & 15 & -16 \\-13 & -1 & 33\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]A C=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 3 & -4 \\1 & 0 & -2 \\1 & -5 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}5 & 2 & -2 \\4 & 5 & -4 \\-5 & 3 & 7\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rr}10+12+20 & 4+15-12 \\5+0+10 & 2+0-6 \\5-20-30 & 2-25+18\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}-4-12-28 \\-2+0-14 \\-2+20+42\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}42 & 7 & -44 \\15 & -4 & -16 \\-45 & -5 & 60\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\mathrm{CA}=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}5 & 2 & -2 \\4 & 5 & -4 \\-5 & 3 & 7\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 3 & -4 \\1 & 0 & -2 \\1 & -5 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rr}10+2-2 & 15+0+10 \\8+5-4 & 12+0+20 \\-10+3+7 & -15+0-35\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}-20-4-12 \\-16-10-24 \\20-6+42\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}10 & 25 & -36 \\9 & 32 & -50 \\0 & -50 & 56\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{AC} 
eq \mathrm{CA}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{AB}=\left[\begin{array}{l}1 \\3 \\2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 3 & -4 \\1 & 0 & -2 \\1 & -5 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}1 \\3 \\2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore\left[\begin{array}{l}2 x+3 y-4 z \\x-2 z \\x-5 y+6 z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}1 \\3 \\2\end{array}\right][/math]
বামপক্ষ ও ডানপক্ষ সমীকৃত করে পাই, [math]2 x+3 y-4 z=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}x-2 z=3 \\x-5 y+6 z=2\end{array}[/math]
x, y ও z এর সহগগুলো দ্বারা গঠিত নির্ণায়ক হবে[math]D=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 3 & -4 \\1 & 0 & -2 \\1 & -5 & 6\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(0-10)-3(6+2)[/math]
 [math]+(-4)(-5-0)[/math]
 [math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 3 & -4 \\3 & 0 & -2 \\2 & -5 & 6\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-20-24+20[/math]
 [math]=-24 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 1 & -4 \\1 & 3 & -2 \\1 & 2 & 6\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(18-10)-3(18+4)[/math]
 [math]+(-4)(-15-0)[/math]
 [math]D_{z}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 3 & 1 \\1 & 0 & 3 \\1 & -5 & 2\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(0+15)-3(2-3)[/math]
 [math]+1(-5-0)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore x=\frac{D_{x}}{D}=\frac{-16}{-24}=\frac{2}{3} \text { (Ans.) } \\\therefore y=\frac{D_{y}}{D}=\frac{40}{-24}=\frac{-5}{3} \text { (Ans.) } \\\therefore \mathrm{z}=\frac{D_{y}}{D}=\frac{28}{-24}=\frac{-7}{6} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ক [math]2A+3C= \begin{pmatrix}49 & 12 & -14\\14 & 15 & -16\\-13 & -1 & 33\end{pmatrix}[/math]; কারণ স্কেলার দ্বারা গুণ করার পরে সমমানের উপাদানগুলো যোগ করা হয়। 

খ [math]AC=\begin{pmatrix}62 & 7 & -44\\25 & -4 & -16\\-35 & -5 & 60\end{pmatrix},\quad CA=\begin{pmatrix}30 & 55 & -76\\9 & 32 & -50\\0 & -50 & 56\end{pmatrix}[/math]; যেহেতু, উদাহরণস্বরূপ [math]AC_{11}=62\neq CA_{11}=30[/math], তাই [math]AC\neq CA[/math] — ম্যাট্রিক্স গুণ সাধারণত কমিউটেটিভ নয়। 

গ det([math]A[/math]) = [math]-24\neq0[/math], তাই Cramer পদ্ধতি প্রয়োগযোগ্য; [math]D_x=-16,\;D_y=40,\;D_z=28[/math] থেকে [math]x=\dfrac{D_x}{\det A}=\dfrac{2}{3},\;y=\dfrac{D_y}{\det A}=-\dfrac{5}{3},\;z=\dfrac{D_z}{\det A}=-\dfrac{7}{6}[/math].

Question #11 (ID: 414832)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rr}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math] এবং [math]f(x)=x^{2}+2 x-8[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]|A+B|[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math](\mathrm{AB})^{-1}=\mathrm{B}^{-1} \mathrm{~A}^{-1}[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{1}{3} \mathrm{f}(\mathrm{A})[/math] একটি অভেদ ম্যাট্রিক্স।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]A+B=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}3 & 2 \\5 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore|A+B|=\left|\begin{array}{ll}3 & 2 \\5 & -1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-3-10=-13 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\mathrm{AB}=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ll}2, & 0 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}2+2 & 0+4 \\8-3 & 0-6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}4 & 4 \\5 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]|A|=\left|\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-3-8=-11[/math]
 [math]A_{11}=(-1)^{1+1}(-3)=-3 ;[/math]
 [math]A_{12}=(-1)^{1+2}(4)=-4[/math]
 [math]A_{21}=(-1)^{2+1}(2)=-2 ;[/math]
 [math]A_{22}=(-1)^{2+2}(1)=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}^{-1}=\frac{1}{|\mathrm{~A}|} \operatorname{adj} \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{-11}\left[\begin{array}{ll}\mathrm{A}_{11} & \mathrm{~A}_{12} \\\mathrm{~A}_{21} & \mathrm{~A}_{22}\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{t}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{11}\left[\begin{array}{cc}\mathrm{A}_{11} & \mathrm{~A}_{21} \\\mathrm{~A}_{12} & \mathrm{~A}_{22}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{11}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-3 & -2 \\-4 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
অনুরূপভাবে, [math]\mathrm{B}^{-1}=\frac{1}{4-0}\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 0 \\-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 0 \\-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math](\mathrm{AB})^{-1}=\frac{1}{-24-20}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-6 & -4 \\-5 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{-44}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-6 & -4 \\-5 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]
আবার, [math]\mathrm{B}^{-1} \mathrm{~A}^{-1}=\frac{1}{4}\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 0 \\-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{-1}{11}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-3 & -2 \\-4 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{44}\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 0 \\-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}-3 & -2 \\-4 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{44}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-6-0 & -4+0 \\3-8 & 2+2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{44}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-6 & -4 \\-5 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore(\mathrm{AB})^{-1}=\mathrm{B}^{-1} \mathrm{~A}^{-1}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে [math]f(x)=x^{2}+2 x-8[/math]
 [math]\therefore f(A)=A^{2}+2 A-8 I[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+2\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-8\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1+8 & 2-6 \\-4-12 & 8+9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 4 \\8 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{cc}8 & 0 \\0 & 8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}9 & -4 \\-8 & 17\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 4 \\8 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{cc}8 & 0 \\0 & 8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}9+2-8 & -4+4-0 \\-8+8-0 & 17-6-8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & 0 \\0 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1}{3} \mathrm{f}(\mathrm{A})=\frac{1}{3}\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & 0 \\0 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1}{3} \mathrm{f}(\mathrm{A})[/math]
 একটি অভেদ ম্যাট্রিক্স । (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক প্রথমে [math]A+B=\begin{pmatrix}3 & 2\\[4pt]5 & -1\end{pmatrix}[/math] তাই [math]|A+B|=3\cdot(-1)-2\cdot5=-3-10=-13[/math]।

খ কারণ [math](AB)(B^{-1}A^{-1})=A(BB^{-1})A^{-1}=AIA^{-1}=I[/math] এবং একইভাবে [math](B^{-1}A^{-1})(AB)=I[/math], ফলে [math]B^{-1}A^{-1}[/math] হল [math]AB[/math] এর অনূর্ধ্ব, অর্থাৎ [math](AB)^{-1}=B^{-1}A^{-1}[/math]।

গ হিসাব করলে [math]A^{2}=\begin{pmatrix}9 & -4\\[4pt]-8 & 17\end{pmatrix}[/math] তাই [math]f(A)=A^{2}+2A-8I=\begin{pmatrix}3 & 0\\[4pt]0 & 3\end{pmatrix}=3I[/math], ফলে [math]\tfrac{1}{3}f(A)=I[/math] যা অভেদ ম্যাট্রিক্স।

Question #12 (ID: 414833)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rr}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math] এবং [math]f(x)=x^{2}+2 x-8[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]|A+B|[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math](\mathrm{AB})^{-1}=\mathrm{B}^{-1} \mathrm{~A}^{-1}[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{1}{3} \mathrm{f}(\mathrm{A})[/math] একটি অভেদ ম্যাট্রিক্স।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]A+B=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}3 & 2 \\5 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore|A+B|=\left|\begin{array}{ll}3 & 2 \\5 & -1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-3-10=-13 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\mathrm{AB}=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ll}2, & 0 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}2+2 & 0+4 \\8-3 & 0-6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}4 & 4 \\5 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]|A|=\left|\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-3-8=-11[/math]
 [math]A_{11}=(-1)^{1+1}(-3)=-3 ;[/math]
 [math]A_{12}=(-1)^{1+2}(4)=-4[/math]
 [math]A_{21}=(-1)^{2+1}(2)=-2 ;[/math]
 [math]A_{22}=(-1)^{2+2}(1)=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}^{-1}=\frac{1}{|\mathrm{~A}|} \operatorname{adj} \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{-11}\left[\begin{array}{ll}\mathrm{A}_{11} & \mathrm{~A}_{12} \\\mathrm{~A}_{21} & \mathrm{~A}_{22}\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{t}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{11}\left[\begin{array}{cc}\mathrm{A}_{11} & \mathrm{~A}_{21} \\\mathrm{~A}_{12} & \mathrm{~A}_{22}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{11}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-3 & -2 \\-4 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
অনুরূপভাবে, [math]\mathrm{B}^{-1}=\frac{1}{4-0}\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 0 \\-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 0 \\-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math](\mathrm{AB})^{-1}=\frac{1}{-24-20}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-6 & -4 \\-5 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{-44}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-6 & -4 \\-5 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]
আবার, [math]\mathrm{B}^{-1} \mathrm{~A}^{-1}=\frac{1}{4}\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 0 \\-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{-1}{11}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-3 & -2 \\-4 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{44}\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 0 \\-1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}-3 & -2 \\-4 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{44}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-6-0 & -4+0 \\3-8 & 2+2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{-1}{44}\left[\begin{array}{cc}-6 & -4 \\-5 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore(\mathrm{AB})^{-1}=\mathrm{B}^{-1} \mathrm{~A}^{-1}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে [math]f(x)=x^{2}+2 x-8[/math]
 [math]\therefore f(A)=A^{2}+2 A-8 I[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+2\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\4 & -3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-8\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1+8 & 2-6 \\-4-12 & 8+9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 4 \\8 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{cc}8 & 0 \\0 & 8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}9 & -4 \\-8 & 17\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{cc}2 & 4 \\8 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{cc}8 & 0 \\0 & 8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}9+2-8 & -4+4-0 \\-8+8-0 & 17-6-8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & 0 \\0 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1}{3} \mathrm{f}(\mathrm{A})=\frac{1}{3}\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & 0 \\0 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1}{3} \mathrm{f}(\mathrm{A})[/math]
 একটি অভেদ ম্যাট্রিক্স । (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]A+B=\begin{pmatrix}3&2\\5&-1\end{pmatrix}[/math] এবং [math]|A+B|=3\cdot(-1)-2\cdot5=-13[/math]।

খ কারণ [math](AB)(B^{-1}A^{-1})=A(BB^{-1})A^{-1}=AIA^{-1}=AA^{-1}=I[/math] এবং অনুরূপভাবে অন্যদিকে গুণ করলেও পরিচয় ম্যাট্রিক্স পাওয়া যায়, তাই [math](AB)^{-1}=B^{-1}A^{-1}[/math]।

গ প্রথমে [math]A^2=\begin{pmatrix}9&-4\\-8&17\end{pmatrix}[/math], তাই [math]f(A)=A^2+2A-8I=\begin{pmatrix}3&0\\0&3\end{pmatrix}=3I[/math], ফলে [math]\tfrac{1}{3}f(A)=I[/math]।

Question #13 (ID: 414834)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}s+c & s-b-c & s-c-a \\s-a-b & s+a & s-c-a \\s-a-b & s-b-c & s+b\end{array}\right][/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}1 & -2 & 3 \\2 & 1 & 2 \\3 & 2 & 1\end{array}\right], C=\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right], F=\left[\begin{array}{l}11 \\10 \\9\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm{B}_{11}+\mathrm{B}_{33}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর যেখানে [math]B_{ij}[/math] হলো [math](i, j)[/math]-তম ভুক্তির সহগুণক ।
খ. [math]s=a+b+c[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]|A|=2(a+b+c)^{3}[/math]
গ. [math]B C=F[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]x+y+z=5[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -2 & 3 \\2 & 1 & 2 \\3 & 2 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]|\mathrm{B}|[/math]
 এর [math](1, 1)[/math]
 তম ভুক্তির সহগুণক[math]\therefore \mathrm{B}_{11}=(-1)^{1+1}\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\2 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1-4=-3[/math]
এবং [math](3, 3)[/math]
 তম ভুক্তির সহগুণক[math]\mathrm{B}_{33}=(-1)^{3+3}\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & -2 \\2 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
=1-(-4)=5$সুতরাং [math]B_{11}+B_{33}[/math]
 [math]=-3+5=2 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]s=a+b+c[/math]
 [math]\therefore|A|=\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}s+c & s-b-c \\s-a-b & s+a \\s-a-b & s-b-c\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}s-c-a \\s-c-a \\ s+b\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}a+b+2 c & a \\c & 2 a+b+c \\c & a\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}b \\b \\ a+2b+c\end{array}\right|[/math]
[s এর মান বসিয়ে ][math]=\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}2(a+b+c) & a \\2(a+b+c) & 2 a+b+c \\2(a+b+c) & a\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}b \\b \\ c+a+2b\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[c_{1}{ }^{\prime}=c_{1}+c_{2}+c_{3}\right.[/math]
 প্রয়োগ করে][math]=2(a+b+c)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & a & b \\1 & 2 a+b+c & b \\1 & a & c+a+2 b\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(a+b+c)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}0 & -(a+b+c) & 0 \\0 & a+b+c & -(a+b+c) \\1 & a & c+a+2 b\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[r_{1}^{\prime}=r_{1}-r_{2}\right.[/math]
 এবং [math]r_{2}^{\prime}=r_{2}-r_{3}[/math]
 প্রয়োগ করে][math]=2(a+b+c)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}-(a+b+c) & 0 \\a+b+c & -(a+b+c)\end{array}\right|[/math]
[প্রথম কলাম সাপেক্ষে বিস্তার করে][math]=2(a+b+c)[/math]
 [math]\left\{(a+b+c)^{2}-0\right\}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=2(a+b+c)^{3} \\\therefore|A|=2(a+b+c)^{3}\end{array}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গপ্রশ্নমতে [math]\mathrm{BC}=\mathrm{F}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -2 & 3 \\2 & 1 & 2 \\3 & 2 & 1\end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{c}11 \\10 \\9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{c}x-2 y+3 z \\2 x+y+2 z \\3 x+2 y+z\end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{c}11 \\10 \\9\end{array}\right][/math]
ম্যাট্রিক্সের সমতা অনুসারে,[math]\begin{array}{l}x-2 y+3 z=11 \\2 x+y+2 z=10 \\3 x+2 y+z=9\end{array}[/math]
এখানে, x, y ও z এর সহগগুচ্ছ নিয়ে গঠিত নির্ণায়ক,[math]\therefore D=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -2 & 3 \\2 & 1 & 2 \\3 & 2 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1(1-4)-(-2)(2-6)[/math]
 [math]+3(4-3)[/math]
 [math]=-3-8+3=-8[/math]
 [math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}11 & -2 & 3 \\10 & 1 & 2 \\9 & 2 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=11(1-4)-(-2)(10-18)[/math]
 [math]+3(20-9)[/math]
 [math]=-33-16+33=-16[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 11 & 3 \\2 & 10 & 2 \\3 & 9 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1(10-18)-11(2-6)[/math]
 [math]+3(18-30)[/math]
 [math]=-8+44-36=0[/math]
 [math]D_{z}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -2 & 11 \\2 & 1 & 10 \\3 & 2 & 9\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1(9-20)-(-2)(18-30)[/math]
 [math]+11(4-3)[/math]
 [math]=-11-24+11=-24[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=\frac{D_{x}}{D}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-16}{-8}=2 ;[/math]
 [math]y=\frac{D_{y}}{D}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{0}{-8}=0 ;[/math]
 [math]z=\frac{D_{z}}{D}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-24}{-8}=3[/math]
সুতরাং [math]x+y+z=2+0+3=5[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
সমাধান:

ক  কফ্যাক্টর নিলে [math]C_{11}=(-1)^{2}\det\begin{pmatrix}1&2\\2&1\end{pmatrix}= -3[/math] এবং [math]C_{33}=(-1)^{6}\det\begin{pmatrix}1&-2\\2&1\end{pmatrix}=5[/math], তাই [math]C_{11}+C_{33}=-3+5=2[/math]।

খ  যদি [math]s=a+b+c[/math] ধরা হয় তাহলে ম্যাট্রিক্সের элементы সরল হয় এবং R2→R2−R3 করলে রো2 হয়ে যায় [math](0,s,-s)[/math]; ডিটারমিনেন্ট গণনায় পরিষ্কারভাবে পাওয়া যায় [math]|A|=s\cdot 2s^{2}=2s^{3}=2(a+b+c)^{3}[/math]।

গ  [math]BC=F[/math] থেকে সমীকরণগুলি যোগ করে প্রথম ও তৃতীয় সমীকরণ যোগ করলে [math]4(x+z)=20[/math] তাই [math]x+z=5[/math]; এটিকে দ্বিতীয় সমীকরণে বসালে [math]2(x+z)+y=10[/math] হয়, ফলে [math]y=0[/math] এবং [math]x+y+z=5[/math]।

Question #14 (ID: 414835)

Question:
[math]P=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}5+a & 6 & 3 \\4 & 3+a & 2 \\1 & 7 & 1+a\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]a=0[/math] হলে [math]|P|[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. ম্যাট্রিক্সটি ব্যতিক্রমী হলে [math]a[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর। !
গ. [math]a=-6[/math] হলে [math]P^{3}+8 P^{2}-20 P-192 I[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে,[math]P=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}5+a & 6 & 3 \\4 & 3+a & 2 \\1 & 7 & 1+a\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]a = 0[/math]
 হলে, [math]P=\left[\begin{array}{lll}5 & 6 & 3 \\4 & 3 & 2 \\1 & 7 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore|P|=\left|\begin{array}{lll}5 & 6 & 3 \\4 & 3 & 2 \\1 & 7 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=5(3-14)-6(4-2)[/math]
 [math]+3(28-3)[/math]
 [math]=-55-12+75=8 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খP ম্যাট্রিক্সটি ব্যতিক্রমী হলে, [math]|\mathrm{P}|=0[/math]
 [math]=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}5+a & 6 & 3 \\4 & 3+a & 2 \\1 & 7 & 1+a\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=0 +3(28-3-a)=0[/math]
 [math]=(5+a)\{(3+a)(1+a)-14\}[/math]
 [math]-6\{4(1+a)-2\}[/math]
 [math]=(a+5)\left(3+3 a+a+a^{2}-14\right)[/math]
 [math]-6(4+4 a-2)[/math]
 [math]+3(25-a)=0[/math]
 [math]=(a+5)\left(a^{2}+4 a-11\right)[/math]
 [math]-6(4 a+2)+75-3 a=0[/math]
 [math]=a^{3}+4 a^{2}-11 a+5 a^{2}[/math]
 [math]+20 a-55-24 a-12+75-3 a[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
 [math]=a^{3}+9 a^{2}-18 a+8=0[/math]
 [math]=a^{3}-a^{2}+10 a^{2}[/math]
 [math]-10 a-8 a+8=0[/math]
 [math]=a^{2}(a-1)+10 a(a-1)[/math]
 [math]-8(a-1)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore(a-1)\left(a^{2}+10 a-8\right)=0[/math]
হয়, [math]a – 1 = 0[/math]
 অথবা, [math]a^{2}+10 a-8=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore a=1 \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore a=\frac{-10 \pm \sqrt{10^{2}-4 \cdot 1 \cdot(-8)}}{2.1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-10 \pm \sqrt{132}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-10 \pm 2 \sqrt{33}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=-5 \pm \sqrt{33}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় a এর মান [math]=1,-5 \pm \sqrt{33}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]a=-6[/math]
 হলে [math]P=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}5-6 & 6 & 3 \\4 & 3-6 & 2 \\1 & 7 & 1-6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-1 & 6 & 3 \\4 & -3 & 2 \\1 & 7 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]P^{2}=P \times P=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-1 & 6 & 3 \\4 & -3 & 2 \\1 & 7 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-1 & 6 & 3 \\4 & -3 & 2 \\1 & 7 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1+24+3 & -6-18+21 \\-4-12+2 & 24+9+14 \\-1+28-5 & 6-21-35\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}-3+12-15 \\12-6-10 \\3+14+25\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}28 & -3 & -6 \\-14 & 47 & -4 \\22 & -50 & 42\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\mathrm{P}^{3}=\mathrm{P}^{2} \times \mathrm{P}=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}28 & -3 & -6 \\-14 & 47 & -4 \\22 & -50 & 42\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-1 & 6 & 3 \\4 & -3 & 2 \\1 & 7 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}-28-12-6 & 168+9-42 \\14+188-4 & -84-141-28 \\-22-200+42 & 132+150+294\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}84-6+30 \\-42+94+20 \\66-100-210\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-46 & 135 & 108 \\198 & -253 & 72 \\-180 & 576 & -244\end{array}\right][/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\mathrm{P}^{3}+8 \mathrm{P}^{2}-20 \mathrm{P}-192 \mathrm{I}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-46 & 135 & 108 \\198 & -253 & 72 \\-180 & 576 & -244\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ccc}224 & -24 & -48 \\-112 & 376 & -32 \\176 & -400 & 336\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-20 & 120 & 60 \\80 & -60 & 40 \\20 & 140 & -100\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-192\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}178 & 111 & 60 \\86 & 123 & 40 \\-4 & 176 & 92\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-20 & 120 & 60 \\80 & -60 & 40 \\20 & 140 & -100\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ccc}192 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 192 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 192\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}198 & -9 & 0 \\6 & 183 & 0 \\-24 & 36 & 192\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ccc}192 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 192 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 192\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}6 & -9 & 0 \\6 & -9 & 0 \\-24 & 36 & 0\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #15 (ID: 414836)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=\left[\begin{array}{lll}a & a^{2} & 1+a^{3} \\b & b^{2} & 1+b^{3} \\c & c^{2} & 1+c^{3}\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -3 & -5 \\-1 & 4 & 5 \\1 & -3 & -4\end{array}\right][/math] ম্যাট্রিক্সটি সমঘাতি কিনা,যাচাই কর ।
খ. [math]a=1, b=-1[/math] ও [math]c=-2[/math] হলে [math]\mathrm{P}^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. দেখাও যে, [math]|P|=(1+a b c)[/math] [math](a-c)(b-a)(b-c)[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কমনে করি [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -3 & -5 \\-1 & 4 & 5 \\1 & -3 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore A^{2}=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -3 & -5 \\-1 & 4 & 5 \\1 & -3 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -3 & -5 \\-1 & 4 & 5 \\1 & -3 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rr}4+3-5 & -6-12+15 \\-2-4+5 & 3+16-15 \\2+3-4 & -3-12+12\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}-10-15+20 \\5+20-20 \\-5-15+16\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -3 & -5 \\-1 & 4 & 5 \\1 & -3 & -4\end{array}\right]=\mathrm{A}[/math]
সুতরাং ম্যাট্রিক্সটি সমঘাতি । (যাচাই করা হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]P=\left[\begin{array}{llll}a & a^{2} & 1+a^{3} \\b & b^{2} & 1+b^{3} \\c & c^{2} & 1+c^{3}\end{array}\right][/math]
এবং [math]a=1, b=-1, c=-2[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \mathrm{P}=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & 2 \\-1, & 1 & 0 \\-2 & 4 & -7\end{array}\right] \\\therefore|\mathrm{P}|=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & 2 \\-1 & 1 & 0 \\-2 & 4 & -7\end{array}\right|\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=1(-7-0)-1(7+0)[/math]
 [math]+2(-4+2)[/math]
 [math]=-7-7-4=-18 
eq 0[/math]
সুতরাং ম্যাট্রিক্সটি বিপরীতযোগ্য[math]\therefore \operatorname{adjP}=\left[\begin{array}{rr}\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 0 \\4 & -7\end{array}\right| & -\left|\begin{array}{rr}-1 & 0 \\-2 & -7\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 2 \\4 & -7\end{array}\right| & \left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 2 \\-2 & -7\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 2 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right| & -\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 2 \\-1 & 0\end{array}\right|\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}\left|\begin{array}{rr}-1 & 1 \\-2 & 4\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 1 \\-2 & 4\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 1 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right|\end{array}\right]^{t}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-7 & -7 & -2 \\15 & -3 & -6 \\-2 & -2 & 2\end{array}\right]^{t}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-7 & 15 & -2 \\-7 & -3 & -2 \\-2 & -6 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{P}^{-1}=\frac{1}{|\mathrm{P}|} \text { adj } \mathrm{P}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{-18}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-7 & 15 & -2 \\-7 & -3 & -2 \\-2 & -6 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{18}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}7 & -15 & 2 \\7 & 3 & 2 \\2 & 6 & -2\end{array}\right]\\\text{(Ans.)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গবামপক্ষ [math]=|P|=\left|\begin{array}{lll}a & a^{2} & 1+a^{3} \\b & b^{2} & 1+b^{3} \\c & c^{2} & 1+c^{3}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\left|\begin{array}{lll}a & a^{2} & 1 \\b & b^{2} & 1 \\c & c^{2} & 1\end{array}\right|+\left|\begin{array}{lll}a & a^{2} & a^{3} \\b & b^{2} & b^{3} \\c & c^{2} & c^{3}\end{array}\right| \\=\left|\begin{array}{lll}a & a^{2} & 1 \\b & b^{2} & 1 \\c & c^{2} & 1\end{array}\right|+a b c\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & a & a^{2} \\1 & b & b^{2} \\1 & c & c^{2}\end{array}\right| \\=\left|\begin{array}{lll}a & a^{2} & 1 \\b & b^{2} & 1 \\c & c^{2} & 1\end{array}\right|-a b c\left|\begin{array}{ccc}a & 1 & a^{2} \\b & 1 & b^{2} \\c & 1 & c^{2}\end{array}\right|\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\left|\begin{array}{lll}a & a^{2} & 1 \\b & b^{2} & 1 \\c & c^{2} & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]+a b c\left|\begin{array}{lll}a & a^{2} & 1 \\b & b^{2} & 1 \\c & c^{2} & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(1+a b c) \left|\begin{array}{ccc}a & a^{2} & 1 \\b & b^{2} & 1 \\c & c^{2} & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(1+a b c)\left|\begin{array}{rrr}a-b & a^{2}-b^{2} & 0 \\b-c & b^{2}-c^{2} & 0 \\c & c^{2} & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}r_{1}^{\prime}=r_{1}-r_{2} \\r^{\prime}{ }_{2}=r_{2}-r_{3}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=(1+a b c)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ll}a-b & (a+b) \\b-c & (b-b) \\b-c) & (b-c)\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(1+a b c)(a-b)(b-c)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & a+b \\1 & b+c\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(1+a b c)(a-b)(b-c)[/math]
 [math](b+c-a-b)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=(1+a b c)(a-b)(b-c)(c-a) \\\therefore|P|=(1+a b c)(a-c)(b-a)(b-c)\end{array}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:

Question #16 (ID: 414837)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}4 & 1 & 5 \\-2 & -1 & -3 \\3 & -4 & -9\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}p^{} & q^{2} & \mathrm{r} \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{2} \\\mathrm{p}^{3}-1 & \mathrm{q}^{3}-1 & \mathrm{r}^{3}-1\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]A[/math] সমঘাতি কিনা যাচাই কর ।
খ. [math]\mathrm{A}^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
গ. দেখাও যে, [math]|\mathrm{B}|=(\mathrm{pqr}-1)(\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q})[/math] [math](\mathrm{q}-\mathrm{r})(\mathrm{r}-\mathrm{p})[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}4 & 1 & 5 \\-2 & -1 & -3 \\3 & -4 & -9\end{array}\right][/math]
A ম্যাট্রিক্স সমঘাতি হবে যদি [math]A^{2}=A[/math]
 হয়।[math]\therefore A^{2}=A \times A=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}4 & 1 & 5 \\-2 & -1 & -3 \\3 & -4 & -9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}4 & 1 & 5 \\-2 & -1 & -3 \\3 & -4 & -9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rr}16-2+15 & 4-1-20 \\-8+2-9 & -2+1+12 \\12+8-27 & 3+4+36\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}20-3-45 \\-10+3+27 \\15+12+81\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}29 & -17,&-28 & \\-15 & 11 & 20 \\-7 & 43 & 108\end{array}\right] 
eq \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}[/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সটি সমঘাতি নয়। [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]|A|=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}4 & 1 & 5 \\-2 & -1 & -3 \\3 & -4 & -9\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=4(9-12)-1(18+9)[/math]
 [math]+5(8+3)[/math]
 [math]=-12-27+55=16 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}^{-1}[/math]
 নির্ণয়যোগ্য[math]\therefore \operatorname{adj} A=\left[\begin{array}{rr}\left|\begin{array}{rr}-1 & -3 \\-4 & -9\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 5 \\-4 & -9\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 5 \\-1 & -3\end{array}\right|\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}- \left.\begin{array}{rr}-2 & -3 \\3 & -9\end{array} \right\rvert\, \\\left|\begin{array}{rr}4 & 5 \\3 & -9\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{rr}4 & 5 \\-2 & -3\end{array}\right|\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{l}\left|\begin{array}{rr}-2 & -1 \\3 & -4\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{rr}4 & 1 \\3 & -4\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{rr}4 & 1 \\-2 & -1\end{array}\right|\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-3 & -27 & 11 \\-11 & -51 & 19 \\2 & 22 & -2\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{t}}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-3 & -11 & 2 \\-27 & -51 & 22 \\11 & 19 & -2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}^{-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{|\mathrm{~A}|} \operatorname{adj} \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{16}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-3 & -11 & 2 \\-27 & -51 & 2 \\11 & 19 & -2\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গবামপক্ষ [math]=|B|=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}p^{2} & q & r \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2} \\p^{3}-1 & q^{3}-1-r^{3}-1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}p_{2} & q_{2} & r^{2} \\p^{3} & q^{2} & r^{2} \\p^{3} & q^{3} & r^{3}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]-\left|\begin{array}{ccc}p_{2} & q_{2} & \mathbf{r} \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2} \\1 & 1 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=p q\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\p & q & r \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]+\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2} \\p & q & r\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=p q r\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\p & q & r \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]-\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\p & q & r \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(p q r-1)\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\p & q & r \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(p q r-1)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}0 & 0 & 1 \\p-q & q-r & r \\p^{2}-q^{2} & q^{2}-r^{2} & r^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[\mathrm{c}_{1}{ }^{\prime}=\mathrm{c}_{1}-\mathrm{c}_{2}, \mathrm{c}_{2}{ }^{\prime}=\mathrm{c}_{2}-\mathrm{c}_{3}\right][/math]
 [math]=(\mathrm{pqr}-1)\left|\begin{array}{cc}\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q} & \mathrm{q}-\mathrm{r} \\(\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q})(\mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q}) & (\mathrm{q}+\mathrm{r})(\mathrm{q}-\mathrm{r})\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(p q r-1)(p-q)(q-r)\left|\begin{array}{cc}1 & 1 \\p+q & q+r\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(\mathrm{pqr}-1)(\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q})[/math]
 [math](\mathrm{q}-\mathrm{r})(\mathrm{q}+\mathrm{r}-\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q})[/math]
 [math]\therefore|\mathrm{B}|=(\mathrm{pqr}-1)(\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q})[/math]
 [math](\mathrm{q}-\mathrm{r})(\mathrm{r}-\mathrm{p})[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
