Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}3 & -4 & 2 \\-2 & 1 & 0 \\-1 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{lll}x & 2 & -2 \\y & 5 & -4 \\z & 7 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]A=\left(\begin{array}{ll}3 & -1 \\2 & -4\end{array}\right)[/math] হলে, [math]A+A^{\mathrm{T}}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]A^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\mathrm{AB}=\mathrm{I}_{3}[/math] থেকে ক্রেমারের সূত্রের সাহায্যে [math](x, y, z)[/math] নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে,[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & -1 \\2 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore A^{\mathrm{T}}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & -1 \\2 & -4\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{T}}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}3 & 2 \\-1 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore A+A^{\mathrm{T}}=\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & -1 \\2 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{cc}3 & 2 \\-1 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}6 & 1 \\1 & -8\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 খউদ্দীপক হতে পাই, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}3 & -4 & 2 \\-2 & 1 & 0 \\-1 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore|A|=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}3 & -4 & 2 \\-2 & 1 & 0 \\-1 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=3(1+0)-(-4)(-2+0)[/math]
 [math]+2(2+1)[/math]
 [math]=3-8+6=9-8=1 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore A^{-1}[/math]
 নির্ণয়যোগ্য[math]\therefore \operatorname{adj} A=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 0 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{rr}-2 & 0 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right| \cdot\left|\begin{array}{lr}-2 & 1 \\-1 & -1\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{ll}-4 & 2 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right| \cdot\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & 2 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & -4 \\-1 & -1\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{rr}-4 & 2 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & 2 \\-2 & 0\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & -4 \\-2 & -1\end{array}\right|\end{array}\right]^t[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 3 \\2 & 5 & 7 \\-2 & -4 & -5\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{t}}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 2 & -2 \\2 & 5 & -4 \\3 & 7 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore A^{-1}=\frac{\operatorname{adj}(A)}{|A|}=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 2 & -2 \\2 & 5 & -4 \\3 & 7 & -5\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গপ্রশ্নমতে, [math]A B=I_{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{ccc}3 & -4 & 2 \\-2 & 1 & 0 \\-1 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{lll}x & 2 & -2 \\y & 5 & -4 \\z & 7 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{c}3 x-4 y+2 z \\-2 x+y+0 . z \\-x-y+z\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}6-20+14 \\-4+5+0 \\-2-5+7\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}-6+16-10 \\4-4+0 \\2+4-5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore\left[\begin{array}{ccc}3 x-4 y+2 z & 0 & 0 \\-2 x+y+0 . z & 1 & 0 \\-x-y+z & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
ম্যাট্রিক্সের সমতা অনুসারে,[math]\begin{array}{l}3 x-4 y+2 z=1 \\-2 x+y+0 . z=0 \\-x-y+z=0\end{array}[/math]
x, y ও z এর সহগগুচ্ছ নিয়ে গঠিত নির্ণায়ক,[math]D =\left|\begin{array}{ccc}3 & -4 & 2 \\-2 & 1 & 0 \\-1 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]= 3(1+0)-(-4)(-2+0)+2(2+1)[/math]
 [math]= 3-8+6=1[/math]
 [math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -4 & 2 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1\left|\begin{array}{cc}1 & 0 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1+0=1[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 1 & 2 \\-2 & 0 & 0 \\1 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-1\left|\begin{array}{rr}-2 & 0 \\1 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-(-2-0)=2[/math]
 [math]D_{z}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}3 & -4 & 1 \\-2 & 1 & 0 \\-1 & -1 & 0\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1\left|\begin{array}{cc}-2 & 1 \\-1 & -1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2+1=3[/math]
 [math]\therefore x =\frac{D_{x}}{D}=\frac{1}{1}=1[/math]
 [math]y^{\prime} =\frac{D y}{D}=\frac{2}{1}=2[/math]
 [math]z =\frac{D_{z}}{D}=\frac{3}{1}=3[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান, [math](x, y, z)=(1,2,3) \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ক যদি [math]A=\begin{pmatrix}3 & -1\\[4pt]2 & -4\end{pmatrix}[/math], তবে [math]A^{\mathrm{T}}=\begin{pmatrix}3 & 2\\[4pt]-1 & -4\end{pmatrix}[/math] এবং তাই [math]A+A^{\mathrm{T}}=\begin{pmatrix}6 & 1\\[4pt]1 & -8\end{pmatrix}[/math].

খ মূল ম্যাট্রিক্সের ডিটারমিন্যান্ট গণনা করলে [math]\det A=3\cdot1-(-4)\cdot(-2)+2\cdot3=1[/math]; ফলে [math]A^{-1}=\operatorname{adj}(A)^{\!}/\det A=\operatorname{adj}(A)[/math] এবং সরাসরি পাওয়া যায় [math]A^{-1}=\begin{pmatrix}1 & 2 & -2\\[4pt]2 & 5 & -4\\[4pt]3 & 7 & -5\end{pmatrix}[/math].

গ [math]\mathrm{AB}=\mathrm{I}_3[/math] হওয়ায় B হলো [math]A^{-1}[/math], তাই প্রথম কলাম [math](x,y,z)^{\mathrm{T}}[/math] হচ্ছে [math]A^{-1}[/math]-এর প্রথম কলাম, অর্থাৎ [math](x,y,z)=(1,2,3)[/math] (এটি ক্রেমারের সূত্র প্রয়োগ করেও পাওয়া যায়)।

Question #65 (ID: 414792)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]P=\left(\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 5 & 3 \\1 & -1 & 6 \\1 & 2 & -5\end{array}\right),[/math] [math]Q=\left(\begin{array}{l}6 \\9 \\0\end{array}\right),[/math] [math]R=\left(\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right)[/math]

Options:
ক. দুইটি ম্যাট্রিক্সের গুণন যোগ্যতা ব্যাখ্যা কর।
খ. [math]f(x)=x^{2}-3 x[/math] হলে [math]f(P)[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\mathrm{P}^{\mathrm{T}} \mathrm{R}=\mathrm{Q}[/math] থেকে প্রাপ্ত সমীকরণ জোটকে নির্ণায়কের সাহায্যে সমাধান কর ৷


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদুইটি ম্যাট্রিক্স [math]A[/math]
 ও [math]B[/math]
 এর গুণফল [math]AB[/math]
 নির্ণয়ের জন্য প্রথম ম্যাট্রিক্স [math]A[/math]
 এর কলাম সংখ্যা ও দ্বিতীয় ম্যাট্রিক্স [math]B[/math]
 এর সারি সংখ্যা সমান হতে হবে । অর্থাৎ [math]\mathrm{A}=\left[\mathrm{a}_{\mathrm{ij}}\right]_{\mathrm{m} \times \mathrm{n}}[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{B}=\left[\mathrm{b}_{\mathrm{ij}}\right]_{\mathrm{n} \times \mathrm{r}}[/math]
 হলে [math]AB[/math]
 নির্ণয় করা সম্ভব।খউদ্দীপক হতে পাই, [math]P=\left(\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 5 & 3 \\1 & -1 & 6 \\1 & 2 & -5\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore P^{2}=P \times P=[/math]
 [math]\left(\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 5 & 3 \\1 & -1 & 6 \\1 & 2 & -5\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]\times\left(\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 5 & 3 \\1 & -1 & 6 \\1 & 2 & -5\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\begin{array}{cc}1+5+3 & 5-5+6 \\1-1+6 & 5+1+12 \\1+2-5 & 5-2-10\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}3+30-15 \\3-6-30 \\3+12+25\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(\begin{array}{rrr}9 & 6 & 18 \\6 & 18 & -33 \\-2 & -7 & 40\end{array}\right)[/math]
আবার, [math]3 P=3 \times\left(\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 5 & 3 \\1 & -1 & 6 \\1 & 2 & -5\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\left(\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 15 & 9 \\3 & -3 & 18 \\3 & 6 & -15\end{array}\right)[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=x^{2}-3 x[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{f}(\mathrm{P})=\mathrm{P}^{2}-3 \mathrm{P}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(\begin{array}{rrr}9 & 6 & 18 \\6 & 18 & -33 \\-2 & -7 & 40\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]-\left(\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 15 & 9 \\3 & -3 & 18 \\3 & 6 & -15\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\begin{array}{rr}9-3 & 6-15 \\6-3 & 18+3 \\-2-3 & -7-6\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}18-9 \\-33-18 \\40+15\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(\begin{array}{rrr}6 & -9 & 9 \\3 & 21 & -51 \\-5 & -13 & 55\end{array}\right) \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গউদ্দীপক হতে পাই,[math]P=\left(\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 5 & 3 \\1 & -1 & 6 \\1 & 2 & -5\end{array}\right),[/math]
 [math]Q=\left(\begin{array}{l}6 \\9 \\0\end{array}\right),[/math]
 [math]R=\left(\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right)[/math]
 [math]\therefore P^{t}=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 5 & 3 \\1 & -1 & 6 \\1 & 2 & -5\end{array}\right]^{t}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & 1 \\5 & -1 & 2 \\3 & 6 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore P^{t} R=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & 1 \\5 & -1 & 2 \\3 & 6 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\times\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{c}x+y+z \\5 x-y+2 z \\3 x+6 y-5 z\end{array}\right][/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]\mathrm{P}^{t} \mathrm{R}=\mathrm{Q}[/math]
 [math]\therefore\left[\begin{array}{c}x+y+z \\5 x-y+2 z \\3 x+6 y-5 z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\9 \\0\end{array}\right][/math]
ম্যাট্রিক্সের সমতা অনুসারে,[math]\begin{array}{l}x+y+z=6 \\5 x-y+2 z=9 \\3 x+6 y-5 z=0\end{array}[/math]
x, y ও z এর সহগগুচ্ছ নিয়ে গঠিত নির্ণায়ক [math]D[/math]
 হলে,[math]\mathrm{D}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & 1 \\5 & -1 & 2 \\3 & 6 & -5\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1(5-12)-1(-25-6)[/math]
 [math]+1(30+3)[/math]
 [math]=-7+31+33=57[/math]
 [math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}6 & 1 & 1 \\9 & -1 & 2 \\0 & 6 & -5\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=6(5-12)-1(-45-0)[/math]
 [math]+1(54+0)[/math]
 [math]=-42+45+54=57[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 6 & 1 \\5 & 9 & 2 \\3 & 0 & -5\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1(-45-0)-6(-25-6)[/math]
 [math]+1(0-27)[/math]
 [math]=-45+186-27=114[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{D}_{\mathrm{z}}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & 6 \\5 & -1 & 9 \\3 & 6 & 0\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1(0-54)-1(0-27)[/math]
 [math]+6(30+3)[/math]
 [math]=-54+27+198=171[/math]
 [math]\therefore x =\frac{D_{x}}{D}=\frac{57}{57}=1[/math]
 [math]y =\frac{D y}{D}=\frac{114}{57}=2[/math]
 [math]z=\frac{D_{z}}{D}=\frac{171}{57}=3[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান [math](x, y, z)=(1,2,3) \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক দুইটি ম্যাট্রিক্স [math]A_{m\times n}[/math] ও [math]B_{p\times q}[/math] গুণনযোগ্য তখনই যখন প্রথমটির কলামের সংখ্যা সমান হয় দ্বিতীয়টির সারির সংখ্যার সাথে, অর্থাৎ [math]n=p[/math]; ফলাফল হবে একটি [math]m\times q[/math] ম্যাট্রিক্স।

খ এখানে [math]f(P)=P^{2}-3P[/math]; প্রথমে [math]P^{2}=\begin{pmatrix}9&6&18\\6&18&-33\\-2&-7&40\end{pmatrix}[/math], [math]3P=\begin{pmatrix}3&15&9\\3&-3&18\\3&6&-15\end{pmatrix}[/math] তাই [math]f(P)=P^{2}-3P=\begin{pmatrix}6&-9&9\\3&21&-51\\-5&-13&55\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

গ [math]P^{T}R=Q[/math] থেকে সারি-কলাম লিখলে সিস্টেমটি হয় [math]x+y+z=6,\;5x-y+2z=9,\;3x+6y-5z=0[/math]। নির্ণায়কের (Cramer) প্রয়োগে মূল নির্ণায়ক [math]D=\det(P^{T})=\det(P)=57[/math], [math]D_{x}=57,\;D_{y}=114,\;D_{z}=171[/math] হওয়ায় [math]x=1,\;y=2,\;z=3[/math]; অতএব [math]R=\begin{pmatrix}1\\2\\3\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

Question #66 (ID: 414793)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 0 & 1 \\3 & 4 & 2 \\2 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]f(x)=x^{2}+3 x-5 I[/math]

Options:
ক. বিস্তার না করিয়া প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\left|\begin{array}{llll}1 & a & a & -2 \\2 & b & b & -4 \\3 & c & c & -6\end{array}\right|[/math] [math]=0[/math]
খ. [math]f(A)[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\mathbf{A}^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত নির্ণায়ক [math]=\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & a & a-2 \\2 & b & b-4 \\3 & c & c-6\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & \mathrm{a} & \mathrm{a} \\2 & \mathrm{~b} & \mathrm{~b} \\3 & \mathrm{c} & \mathrm{c}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]-\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & \mathrm{a} & 2 \\2 & \mathrm{~b} & 4 \\3 & c & 6\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & \mathrm{a} & \mathrm{a} \\2 & \mathrm{~b} & \mathrm{~b} \\3 & \mathrm{c} & \mathrm{c}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]-2\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & \mathrm{a} & 1 \\2 & \mathrm{~b} & 2 \\3 & c & 3\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 0-2.0[/math]
[উভয় নির্ণায়কে দুইটি করে কলাম একই][math]\Rightarrow 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & a & a-2 \\2 & b & b-4 \\3 & c & c-6\end{array}\right|=0[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 0 & 1 \\3 & 4 & 2 \\2 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 এবং [math]f(x)=x^{2}+3 x-5 I[/math]
 [math]\therefore f(A)=A^{2}+3 A-5 I[/math]
এখন, [math], A^{2}=A . A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 0 & 1 \\3 & 4 & 2 \\2 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 0 & 1 \\3 & 4 & 2 \\2 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}4+0+2 & 0+0+1 \\6+12+4 & 0+16+2 \\4+3+6 & 0+4+3\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{l}2+0+3 \\3+8+6 \\2+2+9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}6 & 1 & 5 \\22 & 18 & 17 \\13 & 7 & 13\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore 3 \mathrm{~A}=3[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 0 & 1 \\3 & 4 & 2 \\2 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}6 & 0 & 3 \\9 & 12 & 6 \\6 & 3 & 9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore 5 \mathrm{I}=5[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{lll}5 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 5 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{f}(\mathrm{A})=\mathrm{A}^{2}+3 \mathrm{~A}-5 \mathrm{I}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{rrr}6 & 1 & 5 \\22 & 18 & 17 \\13 & 7 & 13\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{lll}6 & 0 & 3 \\9 & 12 & 6 \\6 & 3 & 9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{lll}5 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 5 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rr}6+6-5 & 1+0-0 \\22+9-0 & 18+12-5 \\13+6-0 & 7+3-0\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}5+3-0 \\17+6-0 \\13+9-5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{rrr}7 & 1 & 8 \\31 & 25 & 23 \\19 & 10 & 17\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 0 & 1 \\3 & 4 & 2 \\2 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore|\mathbf{A}| =\left|\begin{array}{ccc}2 & 0 & 1 \\3 & 4 & 2 \\2 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]= 2(12-2)-0(9-4)+1(3-8)[/math]
 [math]= 20-0-5=15 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore A^{-1}[/math]
 নির্ণয়যোগ্য।[math]\therefore \operatorname{adj}(A)=[/math]
 [math]\begin{bmatrix}\left|\begin{array}{ll}4 & 2 \\1 & 3\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}3 & 2 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}3 & 4 \\2 & 1\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 1 \\1 & 3\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\2 & 1\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 1 \\4 & 2\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\3 & 2\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\3 & 4\end{array}\right|\end{bmatrix}^t[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}10 & -5 & -5 \\1 & 4 & -2 \\-4 & -1 & 8\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{T}}[/math]
 [math]= {\left[\begin{array}{rrr}10 & 1 & -4 \\-5 & 4 & -1 \\-5 & -2 & 8\end{array}\right] }[/math]
 [math]\therefore A^{-1} =\frac{1}{|A|} \operatorname{adj}(A)[/math]
 [math]= \frac{1}{15}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}10 & 1 & -4 \\-5 & 4 & -1 \\-5 & -2 & 8\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ক কারণ দ্বিতীয় এবং তৃতীয় কলাম একই (প্রতিটি [math](a,b,c)^T[/math]) এবং চতুর্থ কলাম প্রথম কলামের [math]-2[/math] গুণ, তাই কলামগুলো লিনিয়ারভাবে নির্ভরশীল; একটি নির্ভরশীল কলাম থাকলে ডিটারমিন্যান্ট শূন্য, সুতরাং [math]=0[/math]। 

খ প্রথমে [math]A^2=[\begin{smallmatrix}6&1&5\\22&18&17\\13&7&13\end{smallmatrix}][/math], এরপর [math]3A=[\begin{smallmatrix}6&0&3\\9&12&6\\6&3&9\end{smallmatrix}][/math] এবং [math]-5I=[\begin{smallmatrix}-5&0&0\\0&-5&0\\0&0&-5\end{smallmatrix}][/math], তাই [math]f(A)=A^2+3A-5I=[\begin{smallmatrix}7&1&8\\31&25&23\\19&10&17\end{smallmatrix}][/math]। 

গ ডিটারমিন্যান্ট [math]\det A=15[/math]; কোফ্যাক্টর-ম্যাট্রিক্সেরTranspose (adjugate) হচ্ছে [math]\operatorname{adj}A=[\begin{smallmatrix}10&1&-4\\-5&4&-1\\-5&-2&8\end{smallmatrix}][/math], সুতরাং [math]A^{-1}=\tfrac{1}{15}\operatorname{adj}A=\tfrac{1}{15}[\begin{smallmatrix}10&1&-4\\-5&4&-1\\-5&-2&8\end{smallmatrix}][/math]।

Question #67 (ID: 414794)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board

Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প: [math]\mathrm{A}\left[\mathrm{a}_{\mathrm{ij}}\right]_{3 \times 3} ;[/math] যেখানে [math]a_{i j}=2 i-j .[/math] [math]I_{3}=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math] এবং [math]f(x)=x^{2}+3 x[/math]

Options:
ক. k-এর কোন মানের জন্য [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}\mathrm{k}+3 & -1 \\k & k+2\end{array}\right][/math] ব্যতিক্রমী হবে ?
খ. [math]f(\mathrm{~A})+2 \mathrm{I}_{3}[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
গ. [math]\left(A+I_{3}\right) \cdot\left(A^{T}-I_{3}\right)[/math] নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}k+3 & -1 \\k & k+2\end{array}\right][/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সটি ব্যতিক্রমী হবে যদি[math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}k+3 & -1 \\k & k+2\end{array}\right|=0[/math]
 হয়[math]= (k+3)(k+2)+[/math]
 [math]k=0[/math]
 [math]= k^{2}+5 k+6+[/math]
 [math]k=0[/math]
 [math]= k^{2}+6 k+6=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore k=\frac{-6 \pm \sqrt{6^{2}-4.1 .6}}{2.1}[/math]
 [math]= \frac{-6 \pm \sqrt{36-24}}{2}[/math]
 [math]= \frac{-6 \pm \sqrt{12}}{2}[/math]
 [math]= \frac{-6 \pm 2 \sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]= -3 \pm \sqrt{3} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[a_{ij}\right]_{3 \times 3}[/math]
 যেখানে এবং [math]a_{ij}=2 i-j[/math]
এবং [math]f(x)=x^{2}+3 x[/math]
 [math]\therefore A=\left[\begin{array}{ll}2.1-1 & 2.1-2 \\2.2-1 & 2.2-2 \\2.3-1 & 2.3-2\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{l}2.1-3 \\2.2-3 \\2.3-3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & -1 \\3 & 2 & 1 \\5 & 4 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore A^{2}=A \cdot A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & -1 \\3 & 2 & 1 \\5 & 4 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & -1 \\3 & 2 & 1 \\5 & 4 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1+0-5 & 0+0-4 \\3+6+5 & 0+4+4 \\5+12+15 & 0+8+12\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{l}-1+0-3 \\-3+2+3 \\-5+4+9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-4 & -4 & -4 \\14 & 8 & 2 \\32 & 20 & 8\end{array}\right][/math]
এখন, [math]\mathrm{f}(\mathrm{A})+2 \mathrm{I}_{3}=\mathrm{A}^{2}+3 \mathrm{~A}+2 \mathrm{I}_{3}[/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}-4 & -4 & -4 \\14 & 8 & 2 \\32 & 20 & 8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+3\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & -1 \\3 & 2 & 1 \\5 & 4 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+2\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}-4 & -4 & -4 \\14 & 8 & 2 \\32 & 20 & 8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 0 & -3 \\9 & 6 & 3 \\15 & 12 & 9\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 2 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rr}-4+3+2 & -4+0+0 \\14+9+0 & 8+6+2 \\32+15+0 & 20+12+0\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}-4-3+0 \\2+3+0 \\8+9+2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -4 & -7 \\23 & 16 & 5 \\47 & 32 & 19\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]A+I_{3}=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & -1 \\3 & 2 & 1 \\5 & 4 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}1+1 & 0+0 & -1+0 \\3+0 & 2+1 & 1+0 \\5+0 & 4+0 & 3+1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 0 & -1 \\3 & 3 & 1 \\5 & 4 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]A^{t}-I_{3}=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & -1 \\3 & 2 & 1 \\5 & 4 & 3\end{array}\right]^{t}-I_{3}[/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 3 & 5 \\0 & 2 & 4 \\-1 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right]-\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1-1 & 3-0 & 5-0 \\0-0 & 2-1 & 4-0 \\-1-0 & 1-0 & 3-1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}0 & 3 & 5 \\0 & 1 & 4 \\-1 & 1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
এখন, [math]\left(A+I_{3}\right) \cdot\left(A^{t}-I_{3}\right)=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 0 & -1 \\3 & 3 & 1 \\5 & 4 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}0 & 3 & 5 \\0 & 1 & 4 \\-1 & 1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{cc}0+0+1 & 6+0-1 \\0+0-1 & 9+3+1 \\0+0-4 & 15+4+4\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}10+0-2 \\15+12+2 \\25+16+8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 5 & 8 \\-1 & 13 & 29 \\-4 & 23 & 49\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক একটি 2×2 মেট্রিক্স ব্যতিক্রমী (singular) হবে যদি তার নির্ণায়ক শূন্য হয়; তাই [math]\det\begin{pmatrix}k+3 & -1 \\ k & k+2\end{pmatrix}=(k+3)(k+2)+k=k^{2}+6k+6=0[/math]. ফলে [math]k=-3\pm\sqrt{3}[/math]।

খ [math]f(A)+2I_3=A^2+3A+2I_3[/math] এবং [math]x^{2}+3x+2=(x+1)(x+2)[/math] থেকে এটি [math](A+I_3)(A+2I_3)[/math] রূপে লিখতে পারি; সরাসরি হিসাব করলে ফলাফল হচ্ছে [math]\begin{pmatrix}1 & -4 & -7 \\ 23 & 16 & 5 \\ 47 & 32 & 19\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

গ প্রথমে [math]A+I_3=\begin{pmatrix}2&0&-1\\3&3&1\\5&4&4\end{pmatrix}[/math] এবং [math]A^{T}-I_3=\begin{pmatrix}0&3&5\\0&1&4\\-1&1&2\end{pmatrix}[/math] গণনা করে গুণ করলে আমরা পাই [math](A+I_3)(A^{T}-I_3)=\begin{pmatrix}1&5&8\\-1&13&29\\-4&23&49\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

Question #68 (ID: 414795)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১: [math]\frac{x}{5}+\frac{3 y}{10}+\frac{z}{10}[/math] [math]=\frac{x}{4}+\frac{y}{4}[/math] [math]=\frac{3 y}{7}[/math] [math]+\frac{4 z}{7}=1[/math]

দৃশ্যকল্প-২: [math]\Delta=\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}(s-x)^{2} & x^{2} \\y^{2} & (s-y)^{2} \\z^{2} & z^{2}\end{array}\right.[/math] [math]\quad[/math] [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}x^{2} \\y^{2} \\ (s-z)^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]

Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rr}2 & 1 \\-2 & -1\end{array}\right][/math] একটি সমঘাতী ম্যাট্রিক্স । ।
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ এ বর্ণিত সমীকরণ জোটটি ক্রেমারের নিয়মে সমাধান কর।
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ এ, যদি [math]s=x+y+z[/math] হয়, তবে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\Delta=2 \mathrm{xyzs}^{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rr}2 & 1 \\-2 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
প্রদত্ত ম্যাট্রিক্সটি সমঘাতি হবে যদি [math]A^{2}=A[/math]
 হয়।[math]\therefore A^{2}=A \cdot A=\left[\begin{array}{rr}2 & 1 \\-2 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rr}2 & 1 \\-2 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rr}4-2 & 2-1 \\-4+2 & -2+1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rr}2 & 1 \\-2 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=A[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}[/math]
 একটি সমঘাতী ম্যাট্রিক্স।(দেখানো হলো )[math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\frac{x}{5}+\frac{3 y}{10}+\frac{z}{10}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{x}{4}+\frac{y}{4}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3 y}{7}+\frac{4 z}{7}=1[/math]
অর্থাৎ, [math]\frac{x}{5}+\frac{3 y}{10}+\frac{z}{10}=1 ;[/math]
 [math]\frac{x}{4}+\frac{y}{4}=1 ;[/math]
 [math]\frac{3 y}{7}+\frac{4 z}{7}=1[/math]
 [math]x, y[/math]
 ও z এর সহগগুচ্ছ নিয়ে গঠিত নির্ণায়ক D হলে,[math]D=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\frac{1}{5} & \frac{3}{10} & \frac{1}{10} \\\frac{1}{4} & \frac{1}{4} & 0 \\0 & \frac{3}{7} & \frac{4}{7}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{5}\left(\frac{1}{4} \cdot \frac{4}{7}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]-\frac{3}{10}\left(\frac{1}{4} \cdot \frac{4}{7}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{10}\left(\frac{1}{4} \frac{3}{7}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{35}-\frac{3}{70}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{3}{280}=\frac{8-12+3}{280}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{280}[/math]
এখন, [math]\mathrm{D}_{\mathrm{x}}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & \frac{3}{10} & \frac{1}{10} \\1 & \frac{1}{4} & 0 \\1 & \frac{3}{7} & \frac{4}{7}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1\left(\frac{1}{4} \cdot \frac{4}{7}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]-\frac{3}{10}\left(\frac{4}{7}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{10}\left(\frac{3}{7}-\frac{1}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{7}-\frac{12}{70}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{10}\left(\frac{12-7}{28}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{40-48+5}{280}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{3}{280}[/math]
আবার, [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\frac{1}{5} & 1 & \frac{1}{10} \\\frac{1}{4} & 1 & 0 \\0 & 1 & \frac{4}{7}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{5}\left(\frac{4}{7}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]-1\left(\frac{1}{4} \frac{4}{7}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{10}\left(\frac{1}{4}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{4}{35}-\frac{1}{7}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{40}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{32-40+7}{280}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{280}[/math]
এবং [math]D_{z}=\left|\begin{array}{lll}\frac{1}{5} & \frac{3}{10} & 1 \\\frac{1}{4} & \frac{1}{4} & 1 \\0 & \frac{3}{7} & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{5}\left(\frac{1}{4}-\frac{3}{7}\right)[/math]
 [math]-\frac{3}{10}\left(\frac{1}{4}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]+1\left(\frac{1}{4} \frac{3}{7}-0\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{5}\left(\frac{7-12}{28}\right)-\frac{3}{40}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{3}{28}=\frac{-10-21$$+30}{280}=-\frac{1}{280}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad x=\frac{D_{x}}{D}=\frac{-\frac{3}{280}}{-\frac{1}{280}}=3 ;[/math]
 [math]y=\frac{D_{y}}{D}=\frac{-\frac{1}{280}}{1}=1[/math]
 এবং [math]z=\frac{D_{z}}{D}=\frac{-\frac{1}{280}}{-\frac{1}{280}}=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান [math](x, y, z)[/math]
 [math]=(3,1,1) \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]s=x+y+z[/math]
এবং [math]\Delta=\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}(s-x)^{2} & x^{2} \\y^{2} & \left(s-y^{2}\right) \\z^{2} & z^{2}\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}x^{2} \\y^{2} \\ (s-z)^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left\lvert\, \begin{array}{c}(x+y+z-x)^{2} \\y^{2} \\z^{2}\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}x^{2} \\(x+y+z-y)^{2} \\z^{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}x^{2} \\y^{2} \\ (x+y+z-z)^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}(y+z)^{2} & x^{2} \\y^{2} & (x+z)^{2} \\z^{2} & z^{2}\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}x^{2}\\y^{2} \\ (x+y)^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}(y+z)^{2} & x^{2}-(y+z)^{2} \\y^{2} & (x+z)^{2}-y^{2} \\z^{2} & z^{2}-z^{2}\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}x^{2}-(y+z)^{2} \\y^{2}-y^{2} \\ (x+y)^{2}-z^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[C_{2}^{\prime}=C_{2}-C_{1}, C_{3}^{\prime}=C_{3}-C_{1}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left\lvert\, \begin{array}{c}(y+z)^{2} \\y^{2} \\z^{2}\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}(x-y-z)(x+y+z) \\(x+y+z)(x-y+z) \\0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}(x-y-z)(x+y+z) \\0 \\ (x+y-z)(x+y+z)\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(x+y+z)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}(y+z)^{2} & x-y-z \\y^{2} & x-y+z \\z^{2} & 0\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}x-y-z \\0 \\ x+y-z\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(x+y+z)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{c}(y+z)^{2}-y^{2}-z^{2} \\y^{2} \\z^{2}\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}x-y-z-x+y-z \\x-y+z \\0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}x-y-z-x-y+z \\0 \\ x+y-z\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[R_{1}^{\prime}=R_{1}-R_{2}-R_{3}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (x+y+z)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}2 y z & -2 z & -2 y \\y^{2} & x-y+z & 0 \\z^{2} & 0 & x+y-z\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2(x+y+z)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}y z & -z & -y \\y^{2} & x-y+z & 0 \\z^{2} & 0 & x+y-z\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2(x+y+z)^{2}}{y z}[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}y z & -y z & -y z \\y^{2} & y(x-y+z) & 0 \\z^{2} & 0 & z(x+y-z)\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2 y^{2} z^{2}(x+y+z)^{2}}{y z}[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & -1 & -1 \\y & x-y+z & 0 \\z & 0 & x+y-z\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 y z(x+y+z)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 0 & 0 \\y & x+z & y \\z & z & x+y\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[C_{2}^{\prime}=C_{1}+C_{2}\right.[/math]
 এবং [math]\left.C_{3}^{\prime}=C_{1}^{\prime}+C_{3}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 y z(x+y+z)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\left(x^{2}+x y+z x+y z-y z\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 y z(x+y+z)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\cdot x(x+y+z)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 x y z(x+y+z)^{3}[/math]
 [math]=2 x y z s^{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \Delta=2 x y z s^{3}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #69 (ID: 414796)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প: [math]\left.\begin{array}{l}x+y+z=3 \\x+a y+a^{2} z=\ell \\x+a^{2} y+a^{4} z=m\end{array}\right\},[/math] [math]{C}=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 2 \\& 0 \\3 & 0\end{array}\right][/math] [math]f(x)=x^{2}+3 x-7[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর: [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}x+y & 3(y+z) & z+x \\1 & 3 & 1 \\z & 3 x & y\end{array}\right|[/math] [math]=0[/math]
খ. সমীকরণগুলোকে [math]AX = B[/math] আকারে প্রকাশ করে, দেখাও যে, [math]\operatorname{Det}(A)=a(a-1)^{2}\left(a^{2}-1\right)[/math]
গ. [math]f(\mathrm{C})[/math] নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবামপক্ষ,[math]=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}x+y & 3(y+z) & z+x \\1 & 3 & 1 \\z & 3 x & y\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}x+y+z & 3 y+3 z+3 x \\1 & 3 \\z & 3 x\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c|c}z+x+y \\1 \\y\end{array} \right\rvert\,\quad[/math]
 [math]\left[\mathrm{R}_{1}^{\prime}=\mathrm{R}_{1}+\mathrm{R}_{3}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left\lvert\, \begin{array}{cc}x+y+z & 3(x+y+z) \\1 & 3 \\z & 3 x\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}y \\x+y+z \\ y\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3(x+y+z)\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\1 & 1 & 1 \\z & x & y\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3(x+y+z) \times 0[/math]
 [কোনো নির্ণায়কের দুইটি সারি (বা কলাম)একই হলে নির্ণায়কের মান শূন্য হবে ।][math]\Rightarrow 0=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}x+y & 3(y+z) & z+x \\1 & 3 & 1 \\z & 3 x & y\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 খদৃশ্যকল্পে বর্ণিত সমীকরণ জোট,[math]x+y+z=3[/math]
 [math]\ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]x+a y+a^{2} z=l[/math]
 [math]\ldots \text { (ii) }[/math]
 [math]x+a^{2} y+a^{4} z=m[/math]
 [math]\ldots \text { (iii) }[/math]
(i), (ii) ও (iii) নং সমীকরণ কে [math]AX = B[/math]
 আকারে প্রকাশ করেপাই, [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\1 & \mathrm{a} & \mathrm{a}^{2} \\1 & \mathrm{a}^{2} & \mathrm{a}^{4}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{x} \\\mathrm{y} \\\mathrm{z}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{c}3 \\l \\\mathrm{~m}\end{array}\right][/math]
যেখানে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 1 & 1 \\1 & \mathrm{a} & \mathrm{a}^{2} \\1 & \mathrm{a}^{2} & \mathrm{a}^{4}\end{array}\right],[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{B}=\left[\begin{array}{c}3 \\l \\\mathrm{~m}\end{array}\right][/math]
 এবং [math]x=\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\operatorname{Det}(A)=[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\1 & a & a^{2} \\1 & a^{2} & a^{4}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left|\begin{array}{lll}0 & 0 & 1 \\a-1 & a^{2}-a & a^{2} \\a^{2}-1 & a^{4}-a^{2} & a^{4}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[c_{1}^{\prime}=c_{2}-c_{1}\right.[/math]
 এবং [math]c_{2}^{\prime}=c_{3}-c_{2}[/math]
 প্রয়োগ করে ][math]\Rightarrow \left|\begin{array}{cc}a-1 & a(a-1) \\a^{2}-1 & a^{2}\left(a^{2}-1\right)\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a(a-1)\left(a^{2}-1\right)\left|\begin{array}{cc}1 & 1 \\1 & a\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a(a-1)\left(a^{2}-1\right)(a-1)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow a(a-1)^{2}\left(a^{2}-1\right)=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \operatorname{Det}(A)=a(a-1)^{2}\left(a^{2}-1\right)[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)গদেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=x^{2}+3 x-7[/math]
 এবং [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\3 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore f(C)=C^{2}+3 C-7I_{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\3 & 0\end{array}\right]^{2}[/math]
 [math]+3\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\3 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-7\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\3 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\3 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & 6 \\9 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ll}7 & 0 \\0 & 7\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{ll}1+6 & 2+0 \\3+0 & 6+0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & 6 \\9 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ll}7 & 0 \\0 & 7\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ll}7 & 2 \\3 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{ll}3 & 6 \\9 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{ll}7 & 0 \\0 & 7\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{ll}7+3-7 & 2+6-0 \\3+9-0 & 6+0-7\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rr}3 & 8 \\12 & -1\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক প্রথম সারিটি দ্বিতীয় ও তৃতীয় সারির লিনিয়ার সমন্বয়: দেখা যায় [math](x+y,\,3(y+z),\,z+x)=(x+y+z)(1,3,1)-(z,3x,y)[/math], তাই সারাগুলো লিনিয়ারভাবে নির্ভরশীল এবং [math]\det=0[/math].

খ সমীকরণগুলি লেখলে [math]A=\begin{pmatrix}1&1&1\\1&a&a^2\\1&a^2&a^4\end{pmatrix},\;X=(x,y,z)^T,\;B=(3,\ell,m)^T[/math]. 이는 Vandermonde ধরনে (রশ্মি [math]1,a,a^2[/math]) হওয়ায় [math]\det A=(a-1)(a^2-1)(a^2-a)=a(a-1)^2(a^2-1)[/math]।

গ [math]C=\begin{pmatrix}1&2\\3&0\end{pmatrix}[/math] হলে [math]C^2=\begin{pmatrix}7&2\\3&6\end{pmatrix}[/math], তাই [math]f(C)=C^2+3C-7I=\begin{pmatrix}3&8\\12&-1\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

Question #70 (ID: 414797)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প: [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & 2 \\-2 & 2 & -2 \\-2 & 1 & -6\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=A^{-1},[/math] [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{r}3 \\-2 \\-7\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]X=\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}0 & 7 & 10 \\-7 & 0 & 15 \\-10 & -15 & 0\end{array}\right][/math] ম্যাট্রিক্সটি বিপ্রতিসম কিনা যাচাই কর।
খ. [math]B[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\mathrm{AX}=\mathrm{C}[/math] হলে [math]x, y, z[/math] নির্ণয় কর ৷


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কধরি, [math]P=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}0 & 7 & 10 \\-7 & 0 & 15 \\-10 & -15 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]P[/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সটি বিপ্রতিসম হবে যদি [math]P^{t}=-P[/math]
 হয়।[math]P^{t}=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}0 & 7 & 10 \\-7 & 0 & 15 \\-10 & -15 & 0\end{array}\right]^{t}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}0 & -7 & -10 \\7 & 0 & -15 \\10 & 15 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=-\left[\begin{array}{rrr}0 & 7 & 10 \\-7 & 0 & 15 \\-10 & -15 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=-P[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{P}[/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সটি বিপ্রতিসম। (যাচাই করা হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]A=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & 2 \\-2 & 2 & -2 \\-2 & 1 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\operatorname{Det} A=|A|=[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & 2 \\-2 & 2 & -2 \\-2 & 1 & -6\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]= 1(-12+2)-0(12-4)[/math]
 [math]+2(-2+4)[/math]
 [math]= -10+4[/math]
 [math]=-6 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সটি বিপরীতযোগ্য।এখন,[math]\therefore \operatorname{adj} A=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & -2 \\1 & -6\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}-2 & -2 \\-2 & -6\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{ll}-2 & 2 \\-2 & 1\end{array}\right|\\-\left|\begin{array}{rr}0 & 2 \\1 & -6\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 2 \\-2 & -6\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 0 \\-2 & 1\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{rr}0 & 2 \\2 & -2\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 2 \\-2 & -2\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 0 \\-2 & 2\end{array}\right|\end{array}\right]^t[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-10 & -8 & 2 \\2 & -2 & -1 \\-4 & -2 & 2\end{array}\right]^{t}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-10 & 2 & -4 \\-8 & -2 & -2 \\2 & -1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore B=A^{-1}=\frac{1}{|A|} \text { adj } A[/math]
 [math]= -\frac{1}{6}\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-10 & 2 & -4 \\-8 & -2 & -2 \\2 & -1 & 2\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & 2 \\-2 & 2 & -2 \\-2 & 1 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & 2 \\-2 & 2 & -2 \\-2 & 1 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 এবং [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{r}3 \\-2 \\-7\end{array}\right][/math]
 এবং [math]A X=C[/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & 2 \\-2 & 2 & -2 \\-2 & 1 & -6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\times\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{r}3 \\-2 \\-7\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{c}x+2 z \\-2 x+2 y-2 z \\-2 x+y-6 z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{r}3 \\-2 \\-7\end{array}\right][/math]
ম্যাট্রিক্সের সমতা অনুসারে,' [math]x+2 z=3[/math]
 [math]\ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]-2 x+2 y-2 z=-2[/math]
 [math]\ldots \ldots \text { (ii) }[/math]
 [math]-2 x+y-6 z=-7[/math]
 [math]\ldots \ldots \text { (iii) }[/math]
x, y ও z এর সহগগুচ্ছ নিয়ে গঠিত নির্ণায়ক [math]D[/math]
 হলে,[math]D=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & 2 \\-2 & 2 & -2 \\-2 & 1 & -6\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=-6[/math]
 [‘খ’ হতে প্রাপ্ত][math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 0 & 2 \\-2 & 2 & -2 \\-7 & 1 & -6\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]= 3(-12+2)-0+2[/math]
 [math](-2+14)[/math]
 [math]= -30+24[/math]
 [math]=-6[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 3 & 2 \\-2 & -2 & -2 \\-2 & -7 & -6\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]= 1(12-14)-3(12-4)[/math]
 [math]+2(14-4)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow -2-24+20=-6[/math]
 [math]D_{z}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & 3 \\-2 & 2 & -2 \\-2 & 1 & -7\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]= 1(-14+2)-0+3(-2+4)[/math]
 [math]= -12+6[/math]
 [math]=-6[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=\frac{D_{x}}{D}=\frac{-6}{-6}=1,[/math]
 [math]y=\frac{D_{y}}{D}=\frac{-6}{-6}=1[/math]
এবং [math]z=\frac{D_{z}}{D}=\frac{-6}{-6}=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore(\mathrm{x}, \mathrm{y}, \mathrm{z})[/math]
 [math]=(1,1,1) \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক প্রদত্ত ম্যাট্রিক্সটির প্রতিলিপি নিতে গেলে দেখিবে তার কর্ষল উপাদানগুলো উলটো চিহ্নে-change হয় এবং মূলদিগুলো শূন্য থাকে, তাই [math]M^T=-M[/math] হওয়ায় এটি বিপ্রতিসম (skew-symmetric)।

খ গুণা ও সহ-ফলকের পদ্ধতিতে বা adjugate দিয়ে [math]\det A=-6[/math] পাওয়া যায় এবং ফলে
[math]B=A^{-1}=\frac{1}{-6}\begin{pmatrix}-10&2&-4\\-8&-2&-2\\2&-1&2\end{pmatrix}=
\begin{pmatrix}5/3&-1/3&2/3\\4/3&1/3&1/3\\-1/3&1/6&-1/3\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

গ সমীকরণ থেকে [math]X=A^{-1}C=BC[/math] এবং গুণফল করে পাওয়া যায়
[math]X=\begin{pmatrix}1\\1\\1\end{pmatrix},[/math] অর্থাৎ [math]x=y=z=1[/math]।

Question #71 (ID: 414798)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}1+m & 2 & 3 \\2 & 3+m & 1 \\3 & 1 & 2+m\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\0 \\8\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 1 & 1 \\1 & p & p^{2} \\1 & p^{2} & p^{4}\end{array}\right|[/math] [math]=p(p-1)^{2}\left(p^{2}-1\right)[/math]
খ. [math]\mathrm{m}=0[/math] হলে [math]A^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
গ. [math]\mathrm{AB}=\mathrm{C}[/math] হলে নির্ণায়কের সাহায্যে সমাধান কর, যখন [math]m = 1[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\text { L.H.S }=[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\1 & p & p^{2} \\1 & p^{2} & p^{4}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 0 & 0 \\1 & p-1 & p^{2}-p \\1 & p^{2}-1 & p^{4}-p^{2}\end{array}\right| ;[/math]
 [math]\left[C_{2}^{\prime}=C_{2}-C_{1}, C_{3}^{\prime}=C_{3}-C_{2}\right][/math]
 [math]= 1(p-1)\left(p^{4}-p^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]-\left(p^{2}-p\right)\left(p^{2}-1\right)[/math]
 [math]= (p-1) \cdot p^{2}\left(p^{2}-1\right)[/math]
 [math]-p(p-1)\left(p^{2}-1\right)[/math]
 [math]= (p-1)\left(p^{2}-1\right)\left(p^{2}-p\right)[/math]
 [math]=p(p-1)\left(p^{2}-1\right)(p-1)[/math]
 [math]= p(p-1)^{2}\left(p^{2}-1\right)[/math]
 [math]=\text { R.H.S }[/math]
 [math]\therefore\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\1 & p & p^{2} \\1 & p^{2} & p^{4}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=p^{\prime}(p-1)^{2}\left(p^{2}-1\right)[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)খদেওয়া আছে,[math]A=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}1+m & 2 & 3 \\2 & 3+m & .1 \\3 & 1 & 2+m^{}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]m=0[/math]
 হলে [math]A=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 2 & 3 \\2 & 3 & 1 \\3 & 1 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore|A|=1(6-1)-2(4-3)+3(2-9)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 5-2-21=-18[/math]
 [math]\therefore \operatorname{adj} A=[/math]
 [math]\begin{bmatrix}\left|\begin{array}{ll}3 & 1 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 1 \\3 & 2\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 3 \\3 & 1\end{array}\right|\\-\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 3 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 3 \\3 & 2\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\3 & 1\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 3 \\3 & 1\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 3 \\2 & 1\end{array}\right|\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|\end{bmatrix}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rr}6-1 & -(4-3) \\-(4-3) & (2-9) \\2-9 & -(1-6)\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}2-9 \\-(1-6) \\3-4\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{T}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{ccc}5 & -1 & -7 \\-1 & -7 & 5 \\-7 & 5 & -1\end{array}\right]^{T}=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}5 & -1 & -7 \\-1 & -7 & 5 \\-7 & 5 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore A^{-1}=\frac{1}{|A|}(\text { adj } A)=\frac{1}{-18}[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}5 & -1 & -7 \\-1 & -7 & 5 \\-7 & 5 & -1\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]m=1[/math]
 হলে [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 2 & 3 \\2 & 4 & 1 \\3 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right],[/math]
 [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]
 এবং [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\0 \\8\end{array}\right][/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]A B=C \Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{lll}2 & 2 & 3 \\2 & 4 & 1 \\3 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\0 \\8\end{array}\right][/math]
ক্রেমারের পদ্ধতিতে,[math]\Delta=\left|\begin{array}{lll}2 & 2 & 3 \\2 & 4 & 1 \\3 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(12-1)-2(6-3)[/math]
 [math]+3(2-12)[/math]
 [math]= 22-6-30=-14[/math]
 [math]\Delta_{\mathrm{x}}=\left|\begin{array}{lll}6 & 2 & 3 \\0 & 4 & 1 \\8 & 1 & 3\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=6(12-1)-2(0-8)[/math]
 [math]+3(0-32)[/math]
 [math]= 66+16-96[/math]
 [math]=-14[/math]
 [math]\Delta_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{lll}2 & 6 & 3 \\2 & 0 & 1 \\3 & 8 & 3\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(0-8)-6(6-3)[/math]
 [math]+3(16-0)[/math]
 [math]= -16-18+48=14[/math]
 [math]\Delta_{z}=\left|\begin{array}{lll}2 & 2 & 6 \\2 & 4 & 0 \\3 & 1 & 8\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(32-0)-2(16-0)[/math]
 [math]+6(2-12)[/math]
 [math]= 64-32-60=-28[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=\frac{\Delta_{x}}{\Delta}=\frac{-14}{-14}=1[/math]
 আবার, [math]y=\frac{\Delta_{y}}{\Delta}=\frac{14}{-14}=-1[/math]
 [math]z=\frac{\Delta_{z}}{\Delta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-28}{-14}=2[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান : [math](x, y, z)=(1,-1,2) \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক প্রথম সারা থেকে দ্বিতীয় ও তৃতীয় সারা বাদ দিলে সারি বদল করে ২×২ নির্ণায়ক পাই: [math]\Delta=(p-1)(p^4-1)-(p^2-1)^2=(p^2-1)\{(p-1)(p^2+1)-(p^2-1)\}=(p^2-1)\,p(p-1)^2[/math], ফলে [math]\Delta=p(p-1)^2(p^2-1)[/math]। 

খ [math]m=0[/math] এ [math]A=\begin{pmatrix}1&2&3\\2&3&1\\3&1&2\end{pmatrix}[/math], [math]\det A=-18[/math] এবং adjoint বের করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]\operatorname{adj}A=\begin{pmatrix}5&-1&-7\\-1&-7&5\\-7&5&-1\end{pmatrix}[/math], সুতরাং [math]A^{-1}=\dfrac{1}{-18}\begin{pmatrix}5&-1&-7\\-1&-7&5\\-7&5&-1\end{pmatrix}=\begin{pmatrix}-\tfrac{5}{18}&\tfrac{1}{18}&\tfrac{7}{18}\\[4pt]\tfrac{1}{18}&\tfrac{7}{18}&-\tfrac{5}{18}\\[4pt]\tfrac{7}{18}&-\tfrac{5}{18}&\tfrac{1}{18}\end{pmatrix}[/math].

গ [math]m=1[/math] এ [math]\det A=-14[/math]. Cramer-এর সূত্র প্রয়োগে প্রথম, দ্বিতীয়, তৃতীয় কোলামের স্থলে [math]C[/math] বসিয়ে নির্ণায়কগুলো হয়েছে [math]-14,\,14,\,-28[/math] অনুসারে [math]x=\tfrac{-14}{-14}=1,\;y=\tfrac{14}{-14}=-1,\;z=\tfrac{-28}{-14}=2[/math]।

Question:
[math]P=\left[\begin{array}{c}1+x^{2}-y^{2} \\2 x y \\-2 y\end{array}\right.[/math] [math]\quad[/math] [math]\begin{array}{c}2 x y \\1-x^{2}+y^{2} \\2 x\end{array}[/math] [math]\quad[/math] [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}2 y \\-2 x \\1-x^{2}-y^{2}\end{array}\right][/math]

এবং [math]f(x)=x^{3}-3 x+2 I[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]{A}=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 2 & 3 \\4 & 5 & 6\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{rr}0 & 2 \\1 & 2 \\0 & -1\end{array}\right][/math] হলে [math]BA[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\operatorname{det}(P)=0[/math] হলে' প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x^{2}+y^{2}=-1[/math]
গ. [math]x=1, y=2[/math] হলে [math]f({\mathrm{p}})[/math] নির্ণয় কর, যেখানে $I একটি অভেদক ম্যাট্রিক্স ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে,[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 2 & 3 \\4 & 5 & 6\end{array}\right],[/math]
 [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{rr}0 & 2 \\1 & 2 \\0 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{BA}=\left[\begin{array}{rr}0 & 2 \\1 & 2 \\0 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 2 & 3 \\4 & 5 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}0+8 & 0+10 & 0+12 \\1+8 & 2+10 & 3+12 \\0-4 & 0-5 & 0-6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}8 & 10 & 12 \\9 & 12 & 15 \\-4 & -5 & -6\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]P=\left[\begin{array}{c}1+x^{2}-y^{2} \\2 x y \\-2 y\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}2 x y \\1-x^{2}+y^{2} \\2 x\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}2 y \\-2 x \\1-x^{2}-y^{2}\end{array}\right][/math]
এবং [math]\operatorname{det}(P)=0[/math]
 [math]\operatorname{det}(P)=\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{c}1+x^{2}-y^{2} \\2 x y \\-2 y\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}2 x y \\1-x^{2}+y^{2} \\2 x\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}2y\\-2x \\ 1-x^{2}-y^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left\lvert\, \begin{array}{c}1+x^{2}-y^{2} \\0 \\-y\left(1+x^{2}+y^{2}\right)\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}0 \\1+x^{2}+y^{2} \\x\left(1+x^{2}+y^{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}2y \\-2x \\ 1-x^{2}-y^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[C_{1}^{\prime}=C_{1}+C_{3} {y}\right.[/math]
 এবং [math]\left.C_{2}^{\prime}=C_{2}-C_{3} x\right][/math]
 [math]=\left(1+x^{2}+y^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 0 & 2 y \\0 & 1 & -2 x \\-y . x & 1-x^{2}-y^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\left(1+x^{2}+y^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\left\{1-x^{2}-y^{2}+2 x^{2}-0+2 y(0+y)\right\}[/math]
 [math]=\left(1+x^{2}+y^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\left(1+x^{2}+y^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\left(1+x^{2}+y^{2}\right)^{3}[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]\left(1+x^{2}+y^{2}\right)^{3}=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow1+x^{2}+y^{2}=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore x^{2}+y^{2}=-1[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]P=\left[\begin{array}{c}1+x^{2}-y^{2} \\2 x y \\-2 y\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}2 x y \\1-x^{2}+y^{2} \\2 x\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}2 y \\-2 x \\1-x^{2}-y^{2}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]x=1, y=2[/math]
 হলে,[math]P=\left[\begin{array}{c}1+1^{2}-2^{2} \\2 \times 1 \times 2 \\-2 \times 2\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}2 \times 1 \times 2 \\1-1^{2}+2^{2} \\2 \times 1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}2 \times 2 \\-2 \times 1 \\1-1^{2}-2^{2}\end{array}\right][/math]

 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}-8-8-16 \\16-8+8 \\-16-4+16\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}4 & 16 & -32 \\16 & 28 & 16 \\32 & -16 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore P^{3}=P^{2} \cdot p=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}4 & 16 & -32 \\16 & 28 & 16 \\32 & -16 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-2 & 4 & 4 \\4 & 4 & -2 \\-4 & 2 & -4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{c}-8+64+128 \\-32+112-64 \\-64-64+16\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]

 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}16-32+128 \\64-56-64 \\128+32+16\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{rrr}184 & 16 & 112 \\16 & 208 & -56 \\-112 & 56 & 176\end{array}\right][/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=x^{3}-3 x+2 I[/math]
 [math]\therefore f(P)=P^{3}-3 P+2 I[/math]

Question #73 (ID: 414800)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & -4 & 2 \\-2 & 1 & 0 \\-1 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}x^{2} & x \\-3 & 2\end{array}\right][/math] ব্যতিক্রমী ব্যতিক্রমী ম্যাট্রিক্স হলে x এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]A B=B A=I_{3}[/math] হলে, [math]B[/math] নির্ণয় কর; যেখানে [math]B[/math] একটি [math]3 \times 3[/math] ক্রমের ম্যাট্রিক্স ।
গ. [math]{C}=A^{t}[/math] হলে [math]C^{2}-5 C+6 I[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\left[\begin{array}{cc}x^{2} & x \\-3 & 2\end{array}\right][/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সটি ব্যতিক্রমী হবে যদি [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}x^{2} & x \\-3 & 2\end{array}\right|=0[/math]
 হয়।[math]\Rightarrow 2 x^{2}+3 x=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x(2 x+3)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore {\mathrm{x}}=0[/math]
 অথবা, [math]x(2 x+3)=0[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 x=-3 \\\therefore x=\frac{-3}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় মান, [math]x = 0[/math]
 অথবা [math]\frac{-3}{2} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খযেহেতু [math]A B=B A=I_{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore B=A^{-1}[/math]
 [math]\therefore|A|=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}3 & -4 & 2 \\-2 & 1 & 0 \\-1 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3(1+0)-(-4)[/math]
 [math](-2+0)+2(2+1)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3-8+6=9-8[/math]
 [math]=1 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore {A}^{-1}[/math]
 নির্ণয়যোগ্য[math]\operatorname{adj} \mathrm{A}=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}\left|\begin{array}{rr}1 & 0 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{rr}-2 & 0 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{rr}-4 & 2 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right|\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & 2 \\-1 & 1\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{rr}-4 & 2 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & 2 \\-2 & 0\end{array}\right|\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{l}\left|\begin{array}{rr}-2 & 1 \\-1 & -1\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & -4 \\-1 & -1\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{rr}3 & -4 \\-2 & 1\end{array}\right|\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 3 \\2 & 5 & 7 \\-2 & -4 & -5\end{array}\right]^{t}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & -2 \\2 & 5 & -4 \\3 & 7 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore B=A^{-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\operatorname{adj}(A)}{|A|}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 2 & -2 \\2 & 5 & -4 \\3 & 7 & -5\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]C =A^{t}=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & -4 & 2 \\-2 & 1 & 0 \\-1 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right]^{t}[/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & -2 & -1 \\-4 & 1 & -1 \\2 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore C^{2}=C . C=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & -2 & -1 \\-4 & 1 & -1 \\2 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & -2 & -1 \\-4 & 1 & -1 \\2 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right] .[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{r}9+8-2 \\-12-4-2 \\6+0+2\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{r}-6-2+0 \\8+1+0 \\-4+0+0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}-3+2-1 \\4-1-1 \\-2+0+1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}15 & -8 & -2 \\-18 & 9 & 2 \\8 & -4 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=C^{2}-5 C+6 I[/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}15 & -8 & -2 \\-18 & 9 & 2 \\8 & -4 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-5\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & -2 & -1 \\-4 & 1 & -1 \\2 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+6\left[\begin{array}{lll}1 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 1 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}15 & -8 & -2 \\-18 & 9 & 2 \\8 & -4 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]-\left[\begin{array}{rrr}15 & -10 & -5 \\-20 & 5 & -5 \\10 & 0 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{lll}6 & 0 & 0 \\0 & 6 & 0 \\0 & 0 & 6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left[\begin{array}{r}15-15+6 \\-18+20+0 \\8-10+0\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{r}-8+10+0 \\9-5+6 \\-4-0+0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{r}-2+5+0 \\2+5+0 \\-1-5+6\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}6 & 2 & 3 \\2 & 10 & 7 \\-2 & -4 & 0\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক Matriksটির নির্ণায়ক নির্ণয় করলে [math]\det\begin{pmatrix}x^{2} & x\\ -3 & 2\end{pmatrix}=2x^{2}+3x=x(2x+3)[/math] পাওয়া যায়; যদি ম্যাট্রিক্সটি ব্যতিক্রমী (অর্থাৎ singular) হয় তাহলে [math]\det=0[/math], ফলে [math]x=0[/math] অথবা [math]x=-\tfrac{3}{2}[/math]।

খ যেহেতু [math]AB=BA=I_{3}[/math], তাই [math]B=A^{-1}[/math]। এখানে [math]\det A=1[/math] এবং যোগস্থাপকের পারস্পরিক স্থানান্তর নিয়ে আমরা পাই [math]A^{-1}=\begin{pmatrix}1&2&-2\\2&5&-4\\3&7&-5\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

গ [math]C=A^{t}=\begin{pmatrix}3&-2&-1\\-4&1&-1\\2&0&1\end{pmatrix}[/math] হলে সরাসরি গুনফল ও যোগ করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]C^{2}-5C+6I=\begin{pmatrix}6&2&3\\2&10&7\\-2&-4&0\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

Question #74 (ID: 414801)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]X=\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math] [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -1 & -1 \\1 & 3 & 2 \\3 & -1 & -5\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\1 \\1\end{array}\right][/math]

এবং [math]C=[/math] [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}p & q & r \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2} \\p^{3}-1 & q^{3}-1 & r^{3}-1\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. বিস্তার না করে , [math]\left|\begin{array}{lll}y+z & x & 1 \\z+x & y & 1 \\x+y & z & 1\end{array}\right|[/math] নির্ণায়কের মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]|C|=(p q r-1) \cdot(p-q)(q-r)(r-p)[/math]
গ. [math]A X=B[/math] হলে নির্ণায়কের সাহায্যে [math]X[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\left|\begin{array}{lll}y+z & x & 1 \\z+x & y & 1 \\x+y & z & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{lll}x+y+z & x & 1 \\x+y+z & y & 1 \\x+y+z & z & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[C_{1}^{\prime}=C_{1}+C_{2}\right][/math]
 [math]=(x+y+z)\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & x & 1 \\1 & y & 1 \\1 & z & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]= (x+y+z) 0[/math]
 [কোনো নির্ণায়কের দুইটি সারি (বা কলাম) একই হলে নির্ণায়কের মান শূন্য হবে । ][math]= 0 \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খবামপক্ষ,[math]=|C|=[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{rrr}p & q & r \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2} \\p^{3}-1 & q^{3}-1 & r^{3}-1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left|\begin{array}{ccc}\mathrm{p} & \mathrm{q} & \mathrm{r} \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{2} \\\mathrm{p}^{3} & \mathrm{q}^{3} & \mathrm{r}^{3}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]-\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\mathrm{p} & \mathrm{q} & \mathrm{r} \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{2} \\1 & 1 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\\mathrm{p} & \mathrm{q} & \mathrm{r} \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]+\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{2} \\\mathrm{p} & \mathrm{q} & \mathrm{r}\end{array}\right| .[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\\mathrm{p} & \mathrm{q} & \mathrm{r} \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]-\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & 1 & 1 \\\mathrm{p} & \mathrm{q} & \mathrm{r} \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (p q r-1)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\mathrm{p} & 1 & 1 \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{r} \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(p q r-1)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}0 & 0 & 1 \\p-q & q-r & r \\p^{2}-q^{2} & q^{2}-r^{2} & r^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}C_{1}^{\prime}=C_{1}-C_{2} \\C_{2}^{\prime}=C_{2}-C_{3}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (p q r-1)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}(p-q) & (q-r) \\(p+q)(p-q) & (q+r)(q-r)\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (p q r-1)(p-q)(q-r)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}1 & 1 \\p+q & q+r\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (p q r-1)(p-q)[/math]
 [math](q-r)(r-p)=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore|C|=(p q r-1)(p-q)[/math]
 [math](q-r)(r-p)[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)গদেওয়া আছে,[math]X=\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right],[/math]
 [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\1 \\1\end{array}\right],[/math]
 [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -1 & -1 \\1 & 3 & 2 \\3 & -1 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]A X=B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -1 & -1 \\1 & 3 & 2 \\3 & -1 & -5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}x \\y \\z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\1 \\1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{c}2 x-y-z \\x+3 y+2 z \\3 x-y-5 z\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{l}6 \\1 \\1\end{array}\right][/math]
ম্যাট্রিক্সের সমতা অনুসারে,[math]\begin{aligned}2 x-y-z & =6 \\x+3 y+2 z & =1 \\3 x-y-5 z & =1\end{aligned}[/math]
এখানে, x, y ও z এর সহগগুচ্ছ নিয়ে গঠিত নির্ণায়ক,[math]D=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -1 & -1 \\1 & 3 & 2 \\3 & -1 & -5\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(-15+2)+1(-5-6)[/math]
 [math]-1(-1-9)[/math]
 [math]= -26-11+10[/math]
 [math]=-27[/math]
 [math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}6 & -1 & -1 \\1 & 3 & 2 \\1 & -1 & -5\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]= 6(- 15+2)+1(-5-2)-1(-1-3)[/math]
 [math]=-78-7+4[/math]
 [math]=-81[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}2 & 6 & -1 \\1 & 1 & 2 \\3 & 1 & -5\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(-5-2)-6(-5-6)[/math]
 [math]-1(1-3)[/math]
 [math]= -14+66+2[/math]
 [math]=54[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{D}_{z}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -1 & 6 \\1 & 3 & 1 \\3 & -1 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=2(3+1)+1(1-3)[/math]
 [math]+6(-1-9)[/math]
 [math]= 8-2-60=-54[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=\frac{D_{x}}{D}=\frac{-81}{-27}=3[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{y}=\frac{\mathrm{D}_{\mathrm{y}}}{\mathrm{D}}=\frac{54}{-27}[/math]
 [math]=-2[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{z}=\frac{\mathrm{D}_{z}}{\mathrm{D}}=\frac{-54}{-27}[/math]
 [math]=2[/math]
 [math]\therefore X=\left[\begin{array}{r}3 \\-2 \\2\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]

Question #75 (ID: 414802)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board

Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ll}4 & 3 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right],[/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & \mathrm{n} \\0 & \mathrm{p}\end{array}\right][/math] এবং [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{lll}0 & 1 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0 \\2 & 0 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]P=\left[\begin{array}{r}1 \\-2 \\3\end{array}\right][/math] এবং [math]Q=\left[\begin{array}{lll}-2 & -10\end{array}\right][/math] হলে, [math][\mathrm{PQ}]^{T}[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. [math]\mathrm{AB}=\mathrm{I}[/math] হলে, [math]n[/math] ও [math]p[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।
গ. [math]C^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]P=\left[\begin{array}{r}1 \\-2 \\3\end{array}\right][/math]
 এবং [math]Q=\left[\begin{array}{ll}-2-1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]P Q=\left[\begin{array}{r}1 \\-2 \\3\end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-2 & -1 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 .(-2) & 1 .(-1) & 1.0 \\-2 .(-2) & -2 .(-1) & -2.0 \\3 .(-2) & 3 .(-1) & 3.0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-2 & -1 & 0 \\4 & 2 & 0 \\-6 & -3 & 0\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore[\mathrm{PQ}]^{\mathrm{T}}=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}-2 & 4 & -6 \\-1 & 2 & -3 \\0 & 0 & 0\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খবিশেষ দ্রষ্টব্য: প্রশ্নটি অসঙ্গতিপূর্ণ। কারণ, [math]AB[/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সের প্রথম ভুক্তি [math]\left(a_{11} b_{11}+a_{11} b_{21}=4\right)[/math]
 এবং [math]I[/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সের প্রথম ভুক্তি [math](1)[/math]
 সমান নয়। কিন্তু [math]AB = I[/math]
 হতে হলে অবশ্যই উভয় ম্যাট্রিক্সের = অনুরূপ ভুক্তিগুলো সমান হতে হবে। তাই এখানে [math]b_{11}=\mathbf{1}[/math]
 এর স্থলে [math]b_{11}=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 বিবেচনা করে সমাধান দেওয়া হয়েছে। কিন্তু [math]a_{11}=4[/math]
 এর স্থলে [math]a_{11}=1[/math]
 ধরেও সমাধানটি করা যাবে। সেক্ষেত্রে উত্তর হবে: [math]p = 1[/math]
 এবং [math]n=-3][/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{ll}4 & 3 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right],[/math]
 [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{ll}\frac{1}{4} & \mathrm{n} \\0 & \mathrm{p}\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore A B=\left[\begin{array}{ll}4 & 3 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{ll}\frac{1}{4} & n \\0 & p\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 4 n+3 p \\0 & p\end{array}\right][/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]AB = 1[/math]
 [math]\therefore\left[\begin{array}{cc}1 & 4 n+3 p \\0 & p\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\0 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
উভয় পক্ষ তুলনা করে পাই, [math]4 n+3 p=0 \ldots \ldots[/math]
(i) এবং [math]p=1......[/math]
 (ii)[math]p[/math]
 এর মান সমীকরণ (i) এ বসিয়ে পাই,[math]4 . n+3.1=0 \Rightarrow 4 n-3[/math]
 [math]\therefore n=\frac{-3}{4} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{lll}0 & 1 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0 \\2 & 0 & 4\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore|C|=\left|\begin{array}{lll}0 & 1 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 0 \\2 & 0 & 4\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]= 0 \cdot(2.4-0.0)[/math]
 [math]-1(4.1-2.0)+2(1.0-2.2)[/math]
 [math]=-1.4+2 .(-4)=-4-8[/math]
 [math]=-12 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore C^{-1}[/math]
 নির্ণয়যোগ্য[math]\therefore \operatorname{adjC}=[/math]
 [math]\begin{bmatrix}\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 0 \\0 & 4\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 0 \\2 & 4\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\2 & 0\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\0 & 4\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 2 \\2 & 4\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 1 \\2 & 0\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\2 & 0\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 2 \\1 & 0\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 1 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|\end{bmatrix}^t[/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}8 & -4 & -4 \\-4 & -4 & 2 \\-4 & 2 & -1\end{array}\right]^{\mathrm{t}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot\left[\begin{array}{rrr}8 & -4 & -4 \\-4 & -4 & 2 \\-4 & 2 & -1\end{array}\right],[/math]
 [math]\therefore C^{-1}=\frac{1}{|C|} \operatorname{adjC}=\frac{1}{-12}[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}8 & -4 & -4 \\-4 & -4 & 2 \\-4 & 2 & -1\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক P ও Q এর গুণফল হল একটি [math]3\times2[/math] ম্যাট্রিক্স: [math]PQ=\begin{pmatrix}-2 & -10\\[4pt]4 & 20\\[4pt]-6 & -30\end{pmatrix}[/math] তাই তার Transpose হল [math](PQ)^{T}=\begin{pmatrix}-2 & 4 & -6\\[4pt]-10 & 20 & -30\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

খ সরাসরি গুণ করলে [math]AB=\begin{pmatrix}4 & 4n+3p\\[4pt]0 & p\end{pmatrix}[/math] হয়, যা পরিচয় ম্যাট্রিক্স [math]\mathrm{I}=\begin{pmatrix}1&0\\[4pt]0&1\end{pmatrix}[/math] এর সমান হতে হলে [math]4=1[/math] পাওয়া দরকার; যা অসম্ভব, অতএব কোনো বাস্তব সংখ্যা [math]n[/math] ও [math]p[/math] রয়েছে না যেগুলোতে [math]AB=I[/math] হয়।

গ প্রথমে নির্ণায়ক পাওয়া যায় [math]\det C=-12[/math] এবং কফ্যাক্টর-ম্যাট্রিক্স থেকে adjugate হল [math]\operatorname{adj}C=\begin{pmatrix}8 & -4 & -4\\[4pt]-4 & -4 & 2\\[4pt]-4 & 2 & -1\end{pmatrix}[/math]। তাই [math]C^{-1}=\dfrac{1}{-12}\operatorname{adj}C=\begin{pmatrix}-\tfrac{2}{3} & \tfrac{1}{3} & \tfrac{1}{3}\\[4pt]\tfrac{1}{3} & \tfrac{1}{3} & -\tfrac{1}{6}\\[4pt]\tfrac{1}{3} & -\tfrac{1}{6} & \tfrac{1}{12}\end{pmatrix}[/math]।

Question #76 (ID: 414803)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board

Question:
[math]\left.\begin{array}{c}x+2 y-z=5 \\3 x-y+3 z=7 \\2 x+3 y+z=11\end{array}\right\}[/math] এবং

[math]R=\left[\begin{array}{c}a \\b \\c+a+2 b\end{array}\right.[/math] [math]\quad[/math] [math]\begin{array}{c}b \\b+c+2 a \\a\end{array}[/math] [math]\quad[/math] [math]\left.\begin{array}{c}a+b+2 c \\c \\c\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -2 & 2 \\3 & 4 & 5\end{array}\right][/math] এবং [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 0 & 2 \\-7 & 1 & 8\end{array}\right][/math] হলে [math]2 A+B[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. ক্রেমারের নিয়ম ব্যবহার করে উদ্দীপকে উল্লিখিত সমীকরণ জোটের সমাধান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]|R|=2(a+b+c)^{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -2 & 2 \\3 & 4 & 5\end{array}\right] ;[/math]
 [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 0 & 2 \\-7 & 1 & 8\end{array}\right][/math]
এখন, [math]2 A=2[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{rrr}1 & -2 & 2 \\3 & 4 & 5\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -4 & 4 \\6 & 8 & 10\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 A+B=\left[\begin{array}{rrr}2 & -4 & 4 \\6 & 8 & 10\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]+\left[\begin{array}{rrr}3 & 0 & 2 \\-7 & 1 & 8\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]= \left[\begin{array}{rrr}5 & -4 & 6 \\-1 & 9 & 18\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]x+2 y-z=5[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}3 x-y+3 z=7 \\2 x+3 y+z=11\end{array}[/math]
x, y ও z এর সহগগুচ্ছ নিয়ে গঠিত নির্ণায়ক[math]\mathrm{D}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & -1 \\3 & -1 & 3 \\2 & 3 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1(-1-9)-2(3-6)[/math]
 [math]-1(9+2)[/math]
 [math]= -10+6-11=-15[/math]
 [math]D_{x}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}5 & 2 & -1 \\7 & -1 & 3 \\11 & 3 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=5(-1-9)-2(7-33)[/math]
 [math]-1(21+11)[/math]
 [math]D_{y}=\left|\begin{array}{lrr}1 & 5 & -1 \\3 & 7 & 3 \\2 & 11 & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1 .(7-33)-5(3-6)[/math]
 [math]-1(33-14)[/math]
 [math]= -26+15-19[/math]
 [math]=-30[/math]
 [math]D_{z}=\left|\begin{array}{rrr}1 & 2 & 5 \\3 & -1 & 7 \\2 & 3 & 11\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=1(-11-21)-2[/math]
 [math](33-14)+5(9+2)[/math]
 [math]= -32-38+55=-15[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=\frac{D_{x}}{D}=\frac{-30}{-15}=2,[/math]
 [math]y=\frac{D_{y}}{D}=\frac{-30}{-15}=2[/math]
এবং [math]z=\frac{D_{z}}{D}=\frac{-15}{-15}=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় সমাধান: [math](x, y, z)[/math]
 [math]=(2,2,1) \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে,[math]|R|=\left\lvert\, \begin{array}{c}a \\b \\c+a+2 b\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}b \\b+c+2 a \\a\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}a+b+2 c \\c\\ c\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left\lvert\, \begin{array}{l}2(a+b+c) \\2(a+b+c) \\2(a+b+c)\end{array}\right.[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{c}b \\b+c+2 a \\a\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\quad[/math]
 [math]\left.\begin{array}{ccc}a+b+2 c \\c \\ c\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math];\left[c_{1}^{\prime}=c_{1}+c_{2}+c_{3}\right.[/math]
 প্রয়োগ করে[math]\Rightarrow 2(a+b+c)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & b & a+b+2 c \\1 & b+c+2 a & c \\1 & a & c\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2(a+b+c)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}0 & -(c+2 a) & (a+b+c) \\0 & -(a+b+c) & 0 \\1 & a & c\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math];\left[r_{1}^{\prime}=r_{1}-r_{2}\right.[/math]
 এবং [math]r_{2}^{\prime}=r_{3}-r_{2}[/math]
 প্রয়োগ করে ][math]\Rightarrow 2(a+b+c)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}-(c+2 a) & (a+b+c) \\-(a+b+c) & 0\end{array}\right|[/math]
[প্রথম কলাম সাপেক্ষে বিস্তার করে[math]\Rightarrow 2(a+b+c)(a+b+c)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=2(a+b+c)^{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore|R|=2(a+b+c)^{3}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Question #77 (ID: 414804)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2021 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\left[\begin{array}{cc}4 & 1 \\3 & M\end{array}\right][/math] [math]B=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}p^{2} & q & r \\p^{3} & q^{2} & r^{2} \\p^{3}-1 & q^{3}-1 & r^{3}-1\end{array}\right][/math] এবং [math]C=\left[\begin{array}{lll}0 & 1 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 3 \\3 & 1 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]

Options:
ক. [math]M[/math] এর মান কত হলে [math]A[/math] ম্যাট্রিক্সের ট্রেস [math]5[/math] হবে?
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]|B|=(p q r-1)(p-q)(q-r)(r-p)[/math]
গ. [math]C^{-1}[/math] নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\left[\begin{array}{cc}4 & 1 \\3 & M\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore A[/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সের ট্রেস [math]=M+4[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 5=M+4[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow M=5-4[/math]
 [math]\therefore M=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore M[/math]
 এর মান [math]1[/math]
 হলে [math]A[/math]
 ম্যাট্রিক্সের ট্রেস [math]5[/math]
 হবে। [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]B=[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}p & q & r \\p^{2} & q^{2} & r^{2} \\p^{3}-1 & q^{3}-1 & r^{3}-1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore|\mathbf{B}|=[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\mathrm{p} & \mathrm{q} & \mathrm{r} \\\mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{2} \\\mathrm{p}^{3}-1 & \mathrm{q}^{3}-1 & \mathrm{r}^{3}-1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\mathrm{p} & \mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{p}^{3}-1 \\\mathrm{q} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{3}-1 \\\mathrm{r} & \mathrm{r}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{3}-1\end{array}\right|[/math]
১ম, ২য় ও ৩য় সারিকে যথাক্রমে ১ম, ২য় ও ৩য় কলামে স্থাপন করে][math]\Rightarrow \left|\begin{array}{lll}{p} & \mathrm{p}^{2} & \mathrm{p}^{3} \\\mathrm{q} & \mathrm{q}^{2} & \mathrm{q}^{3} \\\mathrm{r} & \mathrm{r}^{2} & \mathrm{r}^{3}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]-\left|\begin{array}{ccc}p & \mathrm{p}^{2} & 1 \\q & q^{2} & 1 \\r & r^{2} & 1\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \operatorname{pqr}[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{lll}1 & p & p^{2} \\1 & q & q^{2} \\1 & r & r^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]-\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & {p} & \mathrm{p}^{2} \\1 & q & q^{2} \\1 & r^{2} & r^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
[২য় নির্ণায়কে ২য় ও ৩য় কলাম স্থান বিনিময় করার পর ১ম ও ২য় কলাম স্থান বিনিময় করা হয়েছে।][math]\Rightarrow (\mathrm{pqr}-1)\left|\begin{array}{ccc}1 & \mathrm{p} & \mathrm{p}^{2} \\1 & \mathrm{q} & \mathrm{q}^{2} \\1 & \mathrm{r} & \mathrm{r}^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(\mathrm{pqr}-\mathrm{l})[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{ccc}0 & \mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q} & \mathrm{p}^{2}-\mathrm{q}^{2} \\0 & \mathrm{q}-r & \mathrm{q}^{2}-r^{2} \\1 & r & r^{2}\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\left[r_{1}^{\prime}=r_{1}-r_{2}\right.[/math]
 এবং [math]r_{2}^{\prime}=r_{2}-r_{3}[/math]
 প্রয়োগ করে ][math]\Rightarrow ({p q r}-1)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}(\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q}) & \left(\mathrm{p}^{2}-\mathrm{q}^{2}\right) \\(\mathrm{q}-\mathrm{r}) & \left(\mathrm{q}^{2}-\mathrm{r}^{2}\right)\end{array}\right|[/math]
[প্রথম কলাম সাপেক্ষে বিস্তার করে][math]\Rightarrow (p q r-1)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}(p-q) & (p-q)(p+q) \\(q-r) & (q-r)(q+r)\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]=(p q r-1)(p-q)(q-r)[/math]
 [math]\left|\begin{array}{cc}1 & p+q \\1 & q+r\end{array}\right|[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (p q r-1)[/math]
 [math](p-q)(q-r)({q}+r-p-q)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (p q r-1)(p-q)[/math]
 [math](q-r)(r-p) .[/math]
 [math]\therefore|\mathrm{B}|=(\mathrm{pqr}-1)(\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q})(\mathrm{q}-\mathrm{r})\left(\mathrm{r}^{}-\mathrm{p}\right)[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]C^{\prime}=\left[\begin{array}{lll}0 & 1 & 2 \\1 & 2 & 3 \\3 & 1 & 1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore|C|=0(2-3)-1(1-9)[/math]
 [math]+2(1-6)[/math]
 [math]= 8-10=-2 
eq 0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{C}^{-1}[/math]
 নির্ণয়যোগ্য ।[math]\therefore \operatorname{adj} C=[/math]
 [math]\begin{bmatrix}\left|\begin{array}{ll}2 & 3 \\1 & 1\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{cc}1 & 3 \\3 & 1\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\3 & 1\end{array}\right| \\-\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\1 & 1\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 2 \\3 & 1\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 1 \\3 & 1\end{array}\right| \\\left|\begin{array}{ll}1 & 2 \\2 & 3\end{array}\right|-\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 2 \\1 & 3\end{array}\right| \quad\left|\begin{array}{ll}0 & 1 \\1 & 2\end{array}\right|\end{bmatrix}^t[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{rrr}-1 & 8 & -5 \\1 & -6 & 3 \\-1 & 2 & -1\end{array}\right]^{t}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left[\begin{array}{rrr}-1 & 1 & -1 \\8 & -6 & 2 \\-5 & 3 & -1\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\therefore C^{-1}=\frac{1}{|C|} . \operatorname{adjC}=\frac{1}{-2}[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{ccc}-1 & 1 & -1 \\8 & -6 & 2 \\-5 & 3 & -1\end{array}\right] \text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক ট্রেস হলো প্রধান диагোনালের যোগ, তাই [math]\operatorname{tr}(A)=4+M[/math]; [math]4+M=5[/math] হলে [math]M=1[/math].

খ [math]|B|[/math] একটি অ্যান্টিসিমেট্রিক পলিনোমিয়াল এবং এটি [math](p-q)(q-r)(r-p)[/math] দ্বারা বিভাজ্য; মোট ডিগ্রি বিবেচনায় অবশিষ্ট অংশ একটি ডিগ্রি‑3 সমমিত পলিনোম যা [math]pqr=1[/math] হলে শূন্য হয়, অতএব সেই অংশে ঘনটি [math](pqr-1)[/math] থাকে। স্থিরক নির্ণয়ের জন্য [math](p,q,r)=(1,2,3)[/math] রেখে উভয় দিক গণনা করলে ধ্রুবকটি 1 পাওয়া যায়, তাই [math]|B|=(pqr-1)(p-q)(q-r)(r-p)[/math]।

গ প্রথমে [math]\det C=0(2\cdot1-3\cdot1)-1(1\cdot1-3\cdot3)+2(1\cdot1-2\cdot3)=-2[/math] পাওয়া যায়; তারপর সহযোগক ম্যাট্রিক্স নিয়ে [math]C^{-1}=\dfrac{1}{\det C}\operatorname{adj}(C)[/math] হলে
[math]C^{-1}=\begin{pmatrix}\tfrac{1}{2} & -\tfrac{1}{2} & \tfrac{1}{2} \\[4pt] -4 & 3 & -1 \\[4pt] \tfrac{5}{2} & -\tfrac{3}{2} & \tfrac{1}{2} \end{pmatrix}.[/math]
